""" BET BUDDY — Main API v6.0.0 FastAPI backend for the Bet Buddy college football betting intelligence app. """ from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, BackgroundTasks from fastapi.responses import HTMLResponse from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware import logging import os logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format="%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s") log = logging.getLogger(__name__) app = FastAPI( title="Bet Buddy API", description="College football betting intelligence backend", version="6.0.0" ) app.add_middleware( CORSMiddleware, allow_origins=["*"], allow_credentials=True, allow_methods=["*"], allow_headers=["*"], ) def get_opening_line(line): """ Returns opening spread/total/ml if available, falls back to closing. Reflects real pick conditions — we pick off the opening line Sunday. """ return { "spread": line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread"), "over_under": line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under"), "home_moneyline": line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline"), "away_moneyline": line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline"), } def fetch_all(query_builder, page_size: int = 1000) -> list: """Paginate Supabase query to bypass the 1,000-row default limit.""" all_rows = [] offset = 0 while True: batch = query_builder.range(offset, offset + page_size - 1).execute().data or [] all_rows.extend(batch) if len(batch) < page_size: break offset += page_size return all_rows # ── Health ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/") def root(): return {"status": "ok", "service": "Bet Buddy API", "version": "6.0.0"} @app.get("/health") def health(): return {"status": "healthy"} # ── Pipeline Triggers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/studio", response_class=HTMLResponse) def card_studio(): """Bet Buddy Card Studio — screenshot tool for social media cards.""" import os # Try multiple locations to find studio.html candidates = [ os.path.join(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)), "studio.html"), os.path.join(os.getcwd(), "studio.html"), "/app/studio.html", "studio.html", ] for path in candidates: if os.path.exists(path): with open(path, "r") as f: return f.read() # Debug: show what files are available cwd_files = os.listdir(os.getcwd()) app_files = os.listdir("/app") if os.path.exists("/app") else [] return HTMLResponse( f"

Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/models/ensemble/predict") def ensemble_predict(home_team: str, away_team: str, season: int = 2026, week: int = None, neutral_site: bool = False): import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) sp = predict_sp_from_data(home_team, away_team, season, neutral_site, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(home_team, away_team, season, neutral_site, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((home_team, season)) or adv_stats.get((home_team, season - 1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((away_team, season)) or adv_stats.get((away_team, season - 1)) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, neutral_site, conference_game") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) fake_game = { "home_team": home_team, "away_team": away_team, "season": season, "week": week, "neutral_site": neutral_site, "conference_game": False, "start_date": None, } adj = compute_adjustments(fake_game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) # Try to find market lines lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, home_moneyline, away_moneyline, opening_spread, opening_over_under, opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada") .eq("season", season) .ilike("home_team", home_team) ) line = next((r for r in lines_raw if (r.get("away_team") or "").lower() == away_team.lower()), None) result = _combine( home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, line["spread"] if line else None, line["over_under"] if line else None, line["home_moneyline"] if line else None, line["away_moneyline"] if line else None, adj=adj, ) if not result: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Could not generate prediction for {home_team} vs {away_team}") return result except HTTPException: raise except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.post("/models/ensemble/save") def ensemble_save(season: int = 2026): from models.ensemble_model import save_ensemble_predictions saved = save_ensemble_predictions(season) return {"status": "saved", "predictions_saved": saved} # ── Best Bets + Pick of the Week ────────────────────────────────────────────── def _build_potw_explanation(p: dict, score: float) -> str: parts = [] agreement = p.get("spread_agreement", 0) edge = p.get("edge_spread") or 0 parts.append(f"{agreement}/4 models agree, {edge}pt edge vs market on the spread") if p.get("ou_tier") in ("A+", "A"): exp = p.get("exp_havoc_score") or 0 parts.append(f"explosiveness/havoc profile favors the {'over' if exp > 0 else 'under'}") if p.get("ml_tier") == "A+": ml_edge = round((p.get("ml_edge") or 0) * 100, 1) parts.append(f"moneyline has {ml_edge}% edge vs market implied probability") notes = p.get("adj_notes", []) if notes: parts.append(notes[0].lower()) return ". ".join(parts).capitalize() + "." if parts else f"Composite score: {score}." @app.get("/best-bets") def best_bets(season: int = 2026, week: int = None): import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() if week is None: upcoming = fetch_all( db.table("games").select("week") .eq("season", season).is_("home_points", "null") .order("start_date") ) if not upcoming: return {"error": "No upcoming games found", "season": season} week = upcoming[0]["week"] all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, " "neutral_site, conference_game, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r week_games = fetch_all( db.table("games").select("*") .eq("season", season).eq("week", week).order("start_date") ) if not week_games: return {"error": f"No games found for week {week}", "season": season, "week": week} picks = [] for game in week_games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season - 1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season - 1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ht_l = ht.strip().lower() at_l = at.strip().lower() line = (lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None))) _ol = get_opening_line(line) if line else {} mkt_spread = _ol.get("spread") if line else None mkt_total = _ol.get("over_under") if line else None home_ml = _ol.get("home_moneyline") if line else None away_ml = _ol.get("away_moneyline") if line else None pred = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, mkt_spread, mkt_total, home_ml, away_ml, adj=adj) if not pred: continue pred["game_id"] = game["id"] pred["start_date"] = game.get("start_date") if game.get("home_points") is not None: pred["home_points"] = game["home_points"] pred["away_points"] = game["away_points"] pred["actual_margin"] = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) pred["actual_total"] = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) pred["result"] = "home" if pred["actual_margin"] > 0 else "away" picks.append(pred) if not picks: return {"error": "No predictions generated", "season": season, "week": week} spread_bets = sorted( [p for p in picks if p["spread_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and p.get("edge_spread") is not None], key=lambda p: (-p["spread_confidence"], -(p.get("edge_spread") or 0)) ) ou_bets = sorted( [p for p in picks if p["ou_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and p.get("ou_pick") is not None], key=lambda p: (-p["ou_confidence"], -(abs(p.get("exp_havoc_score") or 0))) ) ml_bets = sorted( [p for p in picks if p["ml_tier"] == "A+" and p.get("ml_pick") is not None], key=lambda p: (-p["ml_confidence"], -(p.get("ml_edge") or 0)) ) def potw_score(p): s = 0.0 s += {"A+": 40, "A": 30, "B": 15, "C": 0}.get(p["spread_tier"], 0) s += min(20.0, (p.get("edge_spread") or 0) * 4) s += (p.get("spread_agreement") or 0) * 5 if p["ou_tier"] in ("A+", "A"): s += {"A+": 20, "A": 12}.get(p["ou_tier"], 0) s += min(10.0, abs(p.get("exp_havoc_score") or 0)) if p["ml_tier"] == "A+": s += 15 s += min(10.0, (p.get("ml_edge") or 0) * 50) if p.get("spread_adjustment") and abs(p["spread_adjustment"]) >= 0.5: s += 5 if p.get("week") and p["week"] <= 2: s -= 15 return round(s, 1) scored = [(p, potw_score(p)) for p in picks if p["spread_tier"] in ("A+", "A")] scored.sort(key=lambda x: -x[1]) pick_of_week = None if scored: potw, potw_val = scored[0] pick_of_week = { "game_id": potw["game_id"], "home_team": potw["home_team"], "away_team": potw["away_team"], "start_date": potw["start_date"], "composite_score": potw_val, "spread_tier": potw["spread_tier"], "spread_pick": potw["spread_pick"], "ensemble_spread": potw["ensemble_spread"], "market_spread": potw["market_spread"], "edge_spread": potw["edge_spread"], "ou_tier": potw["ou_tier"], "ou_pick": potw["ou_pick"], "ml_tier": potw["ml_tier"], "ml_pick": potw["ml_pick"], "ensemble_win_prob": potw["ensemble_win_prob"], "spread_agreement": potw["spread_agreement"], "adj_notes": potw.get("adj_notes", []), "why": _build_potw_explanation(potw, potw_val), "actual_margin": potw.get("actual_margin"), "result": potw.get("result"), } def fmt_spread(p): return { "game_id": p["game_id"], "home_team": p["home_team"], "away_team": p["away_team"], "start_date": p["start_date"], "tier": p["spread_tier"], "pick": p["spread_pick"], "ensemble_spread": p["ensemble_spread"], "market_spread": p["market_spread"], "edge": p["edge_spread"], "confidence": p["spread_confidence"], "agreement": p["spread_agreement"], "models": {"sp": p["sp_margin"], "elo": p["elo_margin"], "ppa": p["ppa_margin"], "advanced": p["advanced_margin"]}, "adj_notes": p.get("adj_notes", []), "actual_margin": p.get("actual_margin"), "result": p.get("result"), } def fmt_ou(p): hit = None if p.get("actual_total") is not None and p.get("market_total") is not None: hit = ((p["ou_pick"] == "over" and p["actual_total"] > p["market_total"]) or (p["ou_pick"] == "under" and p["actual_total"] < p["market_total"])) return { "game_id": p["game_id"], "home_team": p["home_team"], "away_team": p["away_team"], "start_date": p["start_date"], "tier": p["ou_tier"], "pick": p["ou_pick"], "ensemble_total": p["ensemble_total"], "market_total": p["market_total"], "edge": p["edge_total"], "exp_havoc_score": p["exp_havoc_score"], "confidence": p["ou_confidence"], "adj_notes": p.get("adj_notes", []), "actual_total": p.get("actual_total"), "hit": hit, } def fmt_ml(p): pick_team = p["home_team"] if p["ml_pick"] == "home" else p["away_team"] ml_odds = p["home_moneyline"] if p["ml_pick"] == "home" else p["away_moneyline"] implied = (p["home_implied_prob"] if p["ml_pick"] == "home" else p["away_implied_prob"]) hit = None if p.get("actual_margin") is not None: hit = (p["ml_pick"] == "home") == (p["actual_margin"] > 0) return { "game_id": p["game_id"], "home_team": p["home_team"], "away_team": p["away_team"], "start_date": p["start_date"], "tier": p["ml_tier"], "pick": pick_team, "ml_odds": ml_odds, "ensemble_win_prob": p["ensemble_win_prob"], "market_implied_prob": round(implied, 4) if implied else None, "edge": round(p["ml_edge"], 4) if p["ml_edge"] else None, "confidence": p["ml_confidence"], "hit": hit, } return { "season": season, "week": week, "games_analyzed": len(picks), "pick_of_the_week": pick_of_week, "spread_bets": {"count": len(spread_bets), "bets": [fmt_spread(p) for p in spread_bets]}, "ou_bets": {"count": len(ou_bets), "bets": [fmt_ou(p) for p in ou_bets]}, "ml_bets": {"count": len(ml_bets), "bets": [fmt_ml(p) for p in ml_bets]}, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/best-bets/week/{week}") def best_bets_by_week(week: int, season: int = 2026): return best_bets(season=season, week=week) @app.get("/pick-of-week") def pick_of_week(season: int = 2026, week: int = None): result = best_bets(season=season, week=week) if "error" in result: return result return { "season": result["season"], "week": result["week"], "pick_of_the_week": result["pick_of_the_week"], } # ── Games & Stats ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/games") def get_games(season: int = 2026, week: int = lines[:3]} @app.get("/models/ensemble/edge-analysis") def ensemble_edge_analysis(): """ Breaks down ATS hit rate by edge range and agreement count. Use this to find the true sweet spots for tier calibration. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import (1,2), (2,3), (3,5), (5,99)] by_havoc = {} for lo, hi in havoc_buckets: bucket = [r for r in results if lo <= r["abs_havoc"] < hi] if bucket: hits = sum(1 for r in bucket if r["hit"]) @app.get("/odds/{home_team}/{away_team}") def get_game_odds(home_team: str, away_team: str): """Get best available odds for a specific game across all books.""" from pipeline.odds_pipeline import get_best_odds_for_game, BOOK_DEEPLINKS, BOOK_APPSTORE odds = get_best_odds_for_game(home_team, away_team) if not odds: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="No odds found for this game") # Enrich with deep links result = dict(odds) for key in ["spread_by_book", "total_by_book", "ml_by_book"]: if result.get(key): for book, data in result[key].items(): data["deeplink"] = BOOK_DEEPLINKS.get(book, "") data["app_store"] = BOOK_APPSTORE.get(book, "") return result @app.get("/odds/all") def get_all_live_odds(): """Get all currently available live odds.""" from pipeline.db Content ─────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/backtest/weekly-results") def weekly_backtest_results(season: int = 2025, min_edge: float = 0.0, max_edge: float = 999.0, min_agreement: int = 0, bet_size: int = 100): """ Returns week-by-week backtest results for content creation. Calculates P&L assuming $100 flat bet on every A+ pick. Optional filters to tighten A+ criteria: min_edge: minimum edge vs market (e.g. 6.0) max_edge: maximum edge vs market (e.g. 20.0) min_agreement: minimum model agreement 1-4 (e.g. 3) Example: /backtest/weekly-results?season=2025&min_edge=6&max_edge=20&min_agreement=3 """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, " "neutral_site, conference_game, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r if (ht, at, s, None) not in lines: lines[(ht, at, s, None)] = r season_games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("season") == season and g.get("home_points") is not None] # Renumber postseason games for display only max_reg_week = max( (g["week"] for g in season_games if g.get("season_type", "regular") != "postseason"), default=15 ) for g in season_games: if g.get("season_type") == "postseason": g["display_week"] = max_reg_week + (g["week"] or 1) else: g["display_week"] = g["week"] # Group by week weeks = sorted(set(g["display_week"] for g in season_games)) BET = bet_size def pnl_spread(hit, odds: int = -110) -> float: """P&L on flat bet at given odds. hit=None means push = $0.""" if hit is None: return 0 # push if hit: return BET * (100 / abs(odds)) if odds < 0 else BET * (odds / 100) return -BET def pnl_ml(hit, odds: int) -> float: if hit is None: return 0 # push if hit: return (odds / 100 * BET) if odds > 0 else (100 / abs(odds) * BET) return -BET weekly_results = [] cumulative_pnl = 0 cumulative_bets = 0 cumulative_hits = 0 for week in weeks: week_games = [g for g in season_games if g["display_week"] == week] week_bets = [] for game in week_games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) mkt_spread = ol["spread"] mkt_total = ol["over_under"] # ── Sharp money signal ───────────────────────────────────── # spread_movement = closing - opening (negative = moved toward home) # If model picks home and line moved toward home (negative) = sharp agrees # If model picks home and line moved away (positive) = sharp disagrees spread_movement = line.get("spread_movement") sharp_agreement = None # True/False/None sharp_magnitude = 0.0 if spread_movement is not None and mkt_spread is not None: ens_spread = r.get("ensemble_spread") if ens_spread is not None: model_pick_home = ens_spread < mkt_spread # Movement toward home = negative number sharp_pick_home = spread_movement < 0 sharp_agreement = (model_pick_home == sharp_pick_home) sharp_magnitude = abs(spread_movement) # Add sharp signal to result dict for downstream use r["sharp_agreement"] = sharp_agreement r["sharp_magnitude"] = sharp_magnitude r["spread_movement"] = spread_movement # Threshold filtering spread_edge = r.get("edge_spread") or 0 spread_agr = r.get("spread_agreement") or 0 ou_edge = abs((r.get("ensemble_total") or 0) - (mkt_total or 0)) if mkt_total else 0 # Spread A+ bet if r["spread_tier"] == "A+" and mkt_spread is not None: if min_edge <= spread_edge <= max_edge and spread_agr >= min_agreement: ens = r["ensemble_spread"] pick_home = ens < mkt_spread pick_margin = actual_margin if pick_home else -actual_margin # Spread from pick team's perspective pick_spread = mkt_spread if pick_home else -mkt_spread push = (actual_margin == -mkt_spread) covered = pick_margin > -pick_spread hit = None if push else covered pick_team = ht if pick_home else at display_spread = f"{pick_team} {mkt_spread if pick_home and mkt_spread < 0 else f'+{abs(mkt_spread)}'}" ens_margin_val = r.get("ensemble_margin") or 0 proj = ens_margin_val if pick_home else -ens_margin_val # Favorite = negative, underdog = positive pick_is_favorite = (pick_home and mkt_spread < 0) or (not pick_home and mkt_spread > 0) proj_display = f"-{abs(proj):.1f}" if pick_is_favorite else f"+{abs(proj):.1f}" actual_display = f"{pick_margin:+d}" week_bets.append({ "type": "Spread", "tier": "A+", "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pick": display_spread, "projection": proj_display, "odds": -110, "hit": hit, "pnl": round(pnl_spread(hit), 2), "actual": actual_display, "sharp_agreement": sharp_agreement, "sharp_magnitude": round(sharp_magnitude, 1), "spread_movement": spread_movement, }) # O/U A+ bet if r["ou_tier"] == "A+" and mkt_total is not None and r.get("ensemble_total"): if min_edge <= ou_edge <= max_edge: pick_over = r["ensemble_total"] > mkt_total actual_ou_push = actual_total == mkt_total hit = None if actual_ou_push else ((actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total)) week_bets.append({ "type": "O/U", "tier": "A+", "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pick": f"{'Over' if pick_over else 'Under'} {mkt_total}", "projection": f"{round(r['ensemble_total'], 1)}", "odds": -110, "hit": hit, "pnl": round(pnl_spread(hit), 2), "actual": str(actual_total), }) # ML A+ bet if r["ml_tier"] == "A+" and r.get("ml_pick"): pick_home_ml = r["ml_pick"] == "home" ml_odds = (get_opening_line(line)["home_moneyline"] if pick_home_ml else get_opening_line(line)["away_moneyline"]) if ml_odds and spread_agr >= min_agreement: hit = (actual_margin > 0) if pick_home_ml else (actual_margin < 0) pick_team = ht if pick_home_ml else at pick_margin_ml = actual_margin if pick_home_ml else -actual_margin ens_margin_val = r.get("ensemble_margin") or 0 proj_ml = (ens_margin_val if pick_home_ml else -ens_margin_val) week_bets.append({ "type": "ML", "tier": "A+", "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pick": f"{pick_team} ML", "projection": f"{proj_ml:+.1f}", "odds": ml_odds, "hit": hit, "pnl": round(pnl_ml(hit, ml_odds), 2), "actual": f"{pick_margin_ml:+d}", }) # Week summary week_pnl = sum(b["pnl"] for b in week_bets) week_hits = sum(1 for b in week_bets if b["hit"]) week_total = len(week_bets) cumulative_pnl += week_pnl cumulative_bets += week_total cumulative_hits += week_hits weekly_results.append({ "week": week, "is_postseason": any(g.get("season_type") == "postseason" for g in week_games), "bets": week_total, "hits": week_hits, "hit_pct": round(week_hits / week_total * 100, 1) if week_total else 0, "week_pnl": round(week_pnl, 2), "cumulative_pnl": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "cumulative_bets": cumulative_bets, "cumulative_hits": cumulative_hits, "cumulative_pct": round(cumulative_hits / cumulative_bets * 100, 1) if cumulative_bets else 0, "bankroll": round(bet_size * 20 + cumulative_pnl, 2), "bets_detail": week_bets, }) # Season summary season_bets = sum(w["bets"] for w in weekly_results) season_hits = sum(w["hits"] for w in weekly_results) return { "season": season, "starting_bankroll": bet_size * 20, "final_bankroll": round(bet_size * 20 + cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_profit": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_bets": season_bets, "total_hits": season_hits, "hit_pct": round(season_hits / season_bets * 100, 1) if season_bets else 0, "roi": round(cumulative_pnl / (season_bets * 100) * 100, 1) if season_bets else 0, "weekly": weekly_results, } except Exception as e: import traceback return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/backtest/potw-results") def potw_backtest_results(season: int = 2025, bet_size: int = 100): """ Returns Pick of the Week results for each week of the season. Calculates P&L assuming $500 bet on the POTW spread pick. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db BET_SIZE = bet_size all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, " "neutral_site, conference_game, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r if (ht, at, s, None) not in lines: lines[(ht, at, s, None)] = r season_games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("season") == season and g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season_type", "regular") != "postseason"] weeks = sorted(set(g["week"] for g in season_games)) def potw_score(r, game): s = 0.0 # Tier is the dominant factor — A+ gets a huge bonus over A tier = r["spread_tier"] s += {"A+": 60, "A": 20, "B": 5, "C": 0}.get(tier, 0) # Edge matters but cap it tightly — we dont want 22pt edges on # massive dogs dominating just because the spread is huge edge = r.get("edge_spread") or 0 s += min(10.0, edge * 2) # Agreement is important — 4/4 models agreeing is a strong signal s += (r.get("spread_agreement") or 0) * 5 # Bonus if O/U and ML also agree if r["ou_tier"] == "A+": s += 10 if r["ml_tier"] == "A+": s += 10 # Small bonus for adjustments applied if r.get("adj_notes"): s += 3 # Penalize early season when model has less data if game.get("week", 99) <= 2: s -= 10 return round(s, 1) potw_weeks = [] cumulative_pnl = 0 wins = 0 losses = 0 for week in weeks: week_games = [g for g in season_games if g["week"] == week] candidates = [] for game in week_games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) mkt_spread = ol["spread"] mkt_total = ol["over_under"] # Score all three bet types and add each as a candidate # Spread if r["spread_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and mkt_spread is not None: score = potw_score(r, game) ens_spread = r["ensemble_spread"] pick_home = ens_spread < mkt_spread push = (actual_margin == -mkt_spread) home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = None if push else (home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered) pick_team = ht if pick_home else at home_is_fav = mkt_spread < 0 abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) pick_display = f"{pick_team} {f'-{abs_spread}' if (pick_home and home_is_fav) or (not pick_home and not home_is_fav) else f'+{abs_spread}'}" candidates.append((score, { "bet_type": "spread", "pick": pick_display, "tier": r["spread_tier"], "hit": hit, "edge": round(r.get("edge_spread") or 0, 1), "agreement": r.get("spread_agreement"), "odds": -110, "ens_spread": round(ens_spread, 1), "mkt_spread": mkt_spread, }, game, line)) # O/U if r["ou_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and mkt_total is not None and r.get("ensemble_total"): ou_score = potw_score(r, game) # same base score # Adjust for O/U specific signals ou_edge = abs((r.get("ensemble_total") or 0) - mkt_total) ou_score += min(10.0, ou_edge * 2) pick_over = r["ensemble_total"] > mkt_total hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) # push on total (exact) if actual_total == mkt_total: hit = None pick_display = f"{'Over' if pick_over else 'Under'} {mkt_total} ({ht} vs {at})" candidates.append((ou_score, { "bet_type": "ou", "pick": pick_display, "tier": r["ou_tier"], "hit": hit, "edge": round(ou_edge, 1), "agreement": r.get("ou_agreement"), "odds": -110, "ens_total": round(r["ensemble_total"], 1), "mkt_total": mkt_total, }, game, line)) # ML — only A+, must have valid odds if r["ml_tier"] == "A+" and r.get("ml_pick"): pick_home_ml = r["ml_pick"] == "home" ml_odds = (get_opening_line(line)["home_moneyline"] if pick_home_ml else get_opening_line(line)["away_moneyline"]) if ml_odds and abs(ml_odds) <= 250: # skip extreme favorites ml_score = potw_score(r, game) ml_score += min(10.0, (r.get("ml_edge") or 0) * 100) # Bonus for underdog ML — more exciting if ml_odds > 0: ml_score += min(8.0, ml_odds / 20) hit = (actual_margin > 0) if pick_home_ml else (actual_margin < 0) if actual_margin == 0: hit = None pick_team = ht if pick_home_ml else at pick_display = f"{pick_team} ML ({'+' if ml_odds > 0 else ''}{ml_odds})" candidates.append((ml_score, { "bet_type": "ml", "pick": pick_display, "tier": r["ml_tier"], "hit": hit, "edge": round(r.get("ml_edge") or 0, 3), "agreement": r.get("spread_agreement"), "odds": ml_odds, }, game, line)) if not candidates: continue candidates.sort(key=lambda x: -x[0]) score, pick_info, game, line = candidates[0] ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) bet_type = pick_info["bet_type"] hit = pick_info["hit"] odds = pick_info["odds"] # P&L based on bet type and odds if hit is None: pnl = 0 # push elif hit: if odds < 0: pnl = round(BET_SIZE * (100/abs(odds)), 2) else: pnl = round(BET_SIZE * (odds/100), 2) else: pnl = -BET_SIZE cumulative_pnl += pnl if hit is None: pass elif hit: wins += 1 else: losses += 1 potw_weeks.append({ "week": week, "is_postseason": game.get("season_type") == "postseason", "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pick": pick_info["pick"], "bet_type": bet_type, "tier": pick_info["tier"], "composite_score": score, "edge": pick_info["edge"], "agreement": pick_info.get("agreement"), "odds": odds, "actual_margin": actual_margin, "actual_total": actual_total, "hit": hit, "pnl": pnl, "cumulative_pnl": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "bankroll": round(BET_SIZE + cumulative_pnl, 2), }) return { "season": season, "bet_size": BET_SIZE, "starting_bankroll": BET_SIZE, "final_bankroll": round(BET_SIZE + cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_profit": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_weeks": len(potw_weeks), "wins": wins, "losses": losses, "hit_pct": round(wins / len(potw_weeks) * 100, 1) if potw_weeks else 0, "roi": round(cumulative_pnl / (len(potw_weeks) * BET_SIZE) * 100, 1) if potw_weeks else 0, "weeks": potw_weeks, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/backtest/parlay-results") def parlay_backtest_results(season: int = 2025): """ Returns weekly parlay results for two strategies: 1. Balanced: best A+ spread + best A+ O/U + best A+ ML (different games) 2. Max Value: top 3 composite score picks regardless of type Both use $100 bet size. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db BET_SIZE = 100 all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, " "neutral_site, conference_game, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, provider") .not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) PROVIDER_PRIORITY = ["Bovada", "consensus", "ESPN Bet", "DraftKings", "FanDuel", "BetMGM"] lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") provider = r.get("provider", "") for key in [(ht, at, s, w), (ht, at, s, None)]: existing = lines.get(key) if existing is None: lines[key] = r else: existing_priority = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == existing.get("provider", "")), 99) new_priority = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == provider), 99) if new_priority < existing_priority: lines[key] = r season_games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("season") == season and g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season_type", "regular") != "postseason"] weeks = sorted(set(g["week"] for g in season_games)) def american_to_decimal(odds: int) -> float: """Convert American odds to decimal multiplier.""" if odds > 0: return 1 + odds / 100 else: return 1 + 100 / abs(odds) def parlay_payout(legs: list, bet: float) -> float: """Calculate parlay payout from list of American odds.""" decimal = 1.0 for odds in legs: decimal *= american_to_decimal(odds) return round(bet * decimal - bet, 2) def composite_score(r, bet_type): """Score a pick for parlay selection.""" s = 0.0 if bet_type == "spread": s += {"A+": 40, "A": 30}.get(r["spread_tier"], 0) s += min(20.0, (r.get("edge_spread") or 0) * 4) s += (r.get("spread_agreement") or 0) * 5 elif bet_type == "ou": s += {"A+": 40, "A": 30}.get(r["ou_tier"], 0) s += min(20.0, abs(r.get("exp_havoc_score") or 0) * 3) s += min(15.0, (r.get("edge_total") or 0) * 2) elif bet_type == "ml": s += {"A+": 40}.get(r["ml_tier"], 0) s += min(20.0, (r.get("ml_edge") or 0) * 100) return round(s, 1) weekly_results = [] bal_cumulative = 0 max_cumulative = 0 bal_wins = bal_losses = 0 max_wins = max_losses = 0 for week in weeks: week_games = [g for g in season_games if g["week"] == week] all_picks = [] # (score, type, pick_dict, hit) for game in week_games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) mkt_spread = ol["spread"] mkt_total = ol["over_under"] # Spread A+ pick if r["spread_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and mkt_spread is not None: ens = r["ensemble_spread"] pick_home = ens < mkt_spread push = (actual_margin == -mkt_spread) home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = None if push else (home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered) pick_team = ht if pick_home else at home_is_fav = mkt_spread < 0 abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) pick_display = f"{pick_team} {f'-{abs_spread}' if (pick_home and home_is_fav) or (not pick_home and not home_is_fav) else f'+{abs_spread}'}" score = composite_score(r, "spread") all_picks.append({ "score": score, "type": "spread", "game": f"{ht} vs {at}", "pick": pick_display, "odds": -110, "hit": hit, "tier": r["spread_tier"], "game_id": game["id"], }) # O/U A+ pick if r["ou_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and mkt_total is not None and r.get("ensemble_total"): pick_over = r["ensemble_total"] > mkt_total hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) score = composite_score(r, "ou") all_picks.append({ "score": score, "type": "ou", "game": f"{ht} vs {at}", "pick": f"{'Over' if pick_over else 'Under'} {mkt_total}", "pick_with_game": f"{'Over' if pick_over else 'Under'} {mkt_total} ({ht} vs {at})", "odds": -110, "hit": hit, "tier": r["ou_tier"], "game_id": game["id"], }) # ML A+ pick if r["ml_tier"] in ("A+", "A") and r.get("ml_pick"): pick_home_ml = r["ml_pick"] == "home" ml_odds = (get_opening_line(line)["home_moneyline"] if pick_home_ml else get_opening_line(line)["away_moneyline"]) if ml_odds: hit = (actual_margin > 0) if pick_home_ml else (actual_margin < 0) pick_team = ht if pick_home_ml else at score = composite_score(r, "ml") all_picks.append({ "score": score, "type": "ml", "game": f"{ht} vs {at}", "pick": f"{pick_team} ML", "odds": ml_odds, "hit": hit, "tier": r["ml_tier"], "game_id": game["id"], }) if len(all_picks) < 3: continue # ── BALANCED PARLAY ────────────────────────────────────────────── # Try spread + O/U + ML first, fill gaps with best remaining A+ picks spread_picks = sorted([p for p in all_picks if p["type"] == "spread"], key=lambda x: -x["score"]) ou_picks = sorted([p for p in all_picks if p["type"] == "ou"], key=lambda x: -x["score"]) ml_picks = sorted([p for p in all_picks if p["type"] == "ml"], key=lambda x: -x["score"]) bal_legs = [] used_games = set() # First pass: try to get one of each type for pool in [spread_picks, ou_picks, ml_picks]: for pick in pool: if pick["game_id"] not in used_games: bal_legs.append(pick) used_games.add(pick["game_id"]) break # Fill remaining legs with best A+ picks of any type from unused games if len(bal_legs) < 3: sorted_all_fill = sorted(all_picks, key=lambda x: -x["score"]) for pick in sorted_all_fill: if len(bal_legs) == 3: break if pick["game_id"] not in used_games: bal_legs.append(pick) used_games.add(pick["game_id"]) # ── MAX VALUE PARLAY ───────────────────────────────────────────── # Top 3 composite score picks from different games sorted_all = sorted(all_picks, key=lambda x: -x["score"]) max_legs = [] used_games_max = set() for pick in sorted_all: if pick["game_id"] not in used_games_max: max_legs.append(pick) used_games_max.add(pick["game_id"]) if len(max_legs) == 3: break if len(bal_legs) < 3 or len(max_legs) < 3: continue # Calculate results def parlay_result(legs): all_hit = all(l["hit"] for l in legs) odds_list = [l["odds"] for l in legs] payout = parlay_payout(odds_list, BET_SIZE) if all_hit else -BET_SIZE combined_decimal = 1.0 for o in odds_list: combined_decimal *= american_to_decimal(o) combined_american = round((combined_decimal - 1) * 100) if combined_decimal >= 2 else round(-100 / (combined_decimal - 1)) return { "legs": legs, "all_hit": all_hit, "payout": payout, "combined_odds": f"+{combined_american}" if combined_american > 0 else str(combined_american), "potential_win": round(parlay_payout(odds_list, BET_SIZE), 2), } bal_result = parlay_result(bal_legs[:3]) max_result = parlay_result(max_legs) bal_cumulative += bal_result["payout"] max_cumulative += max_result["payout"] if bal_result["all_hit"]: bal_wins += 1 else: bal_losses += 1 if max_result["all_hit"]: max_wins += 1 else: max_losses += 1 weekly_results.append({ "week": week, "balanced_parlay": bal_result, "max_value_parlay": max_result, "bal_cumulative_pnl": round(bal_cumulative, 2), "max_cumulative_pnl": round(max_cumulative, 2), "bal_bankroll": round(1000 + bal_cumulative, 2), "max_bankroll": round(1000 + max_cumulative, 2), }) total_weeks = len(weekly_results) return { "season": season, "bet_size": BET_SIZE, "starting_bankroll": 1000, "balanced": { "final_bankroll": round(1000 + bal_cumulative, 2), "total_profit": round(bal_cumulative, 2), "wins": bal_wins, "losses": bal_losses, "hit_pct": round(bal_wins / total_weeks * 100, 1) if total_weeks else 0, "roi": round(bal_cumulative / (total_weeks * BET_SIZE) * 100, 1) if total_weeks else 0, }, "max_value": { "final_bankroll": round(1000 + max_cumulative, 2), "total_profit": round(max_cumulative, 2), "wins": max_wins, "losses": max_losses, "hit_pct": round(max_wins / total_weeks * 100, 1) if total_weeks else 0, "roi": round(max_cumulative / (total_weeks * BET_SIZE) * 100, 1) if total_weeks else 0, }, "total_weeks": total_weeks, "weekly": weekly_results, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/line-coverage") def line_coverage(season: int = 2025): """ Shows betting line coverage by week — how many games have lines vs total games. Helps diagnose missing weeks in backtest endpoints. """ try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, home_points, away_points") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_points", "null") ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, home_moneyline, away_moneyline, provider, opening_spread, opening_over_under, opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) # Index lines by game + week lines_by_game = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() w = r.get("week") key = (ht, at, w) if key not in lines_by_game: lines_by_game[key] = [] lines_by_game[key].append(r.get("provider", "unknown")) # Group games by week from collections import defaultdict weeks = defaultdict(list) for g in games_raw: weeks[g["week"]].append(g) coverage = [] for week in sorted(weeks.keys()): week_games = weeks[week] games_with_lines = 0 games_without_lines = [] providers_seen = set() for g in week_games: ht = g["home_team"].strip().lower() at = g["away_team"].strip().lower() key = (ht, at, week) if key in lines_by_game: games_with_lines += 1 for p in lines_by_game[key]: providers_seen.add(p) else: games_without_lines.append(f"{g['home_team']} vs {g['away_team']}") total = len(week_games) coverage.append({ "week": week, "total_games": total, "games_with_lines": games_with_lines, "games_without_lines": total - games_with_lines, "coverage_pct": round(games_with_lines / total * 100, 1) if total else 0, "providers": sorted(providers_seen), "missing_games": games_without_lines[:5], # first 5 only }) total_games = sum(c["total_games"] for c in coverage) total_covered = sum(c["games_with_lines"] for c in coverage) return { "season": season, "total_games": total_games, "total_with_lines": total_covered, "overall_coverage": round(total_covered / total_games * 100, 1) if total_games else 0, "weeks": coverage, } except Exception as e: import traceback return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/coverage-gaps") def coverage_gaps(season: int = 2025, min_coverage_pct: float = 50.0): """ Returns weeks with insufficient line coverage. Use this to know which weeks need historical odds backfilled. For live season: run POST /admin/odds/refresh weekly to keep lines current. For historical: use The Odds API historical endpoint (requires paid plan) or manually import lines from a CSV for missing weeks. """ try: from pipeline.db import get_db from collections import defaultdict db = get_db() games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, home_points, away_points") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_points", "null") ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, provider") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines_index = set() for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() lines_index.add((ht, at, r.get("week"))) weeks = defaultdict(list) for g in games_raw: weeks[g["week"]].append(g) gaps = [] for week in sorted(weeks.keys()): wg = weeks[week] covered = sum(1 for g in wg if (g["home_team"].strip().lower(), g["away_team"].strip().lower(), week) in lines_index) pct = round(covered / len(wg) * 100, 1) if wg else 0 if pct < min_coverage_pct: gaps.append({ "week": week, "total_games": len(wg), "games_with_lines": covered, "coverage_pct": pct, "status": "CRITICAL" if pct < 25 else "LOW", "note": "No lines found" if covered == 0 else f"Only {covered}/{len(wg)} games have lines", }) return { "season": season, "threshold_pct": min_coverage_pct, "weeks_with_gaps": len(gaps), "gaps": gaps, "recommendation": ( "Deploy The Odds API integration and run POST /admin/odds/refresh " "for current week. For historical gaps, you will need to either: " "(1) use The Odds API historical endpoint (paid plan), or " "(2) import historical lines from a CSV source like covers.com or sportsbookreviewsonline.com" ) } except Exception as e: import traceback return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/odds/backfill-historical") def backfill_historical_odds(season: int = 2025, week: int = None): """ Pulls historical closing lines from The Odds API for an entire season and upserts them into the betting_lines table. Usage: POST /admin/odds/backfill-historical?season=2025 POST /admin/odds/backfill-historical?season=2025&week=6 Requires ODDS_API_KEY environment variable set in Railway. """ import os, time, traceback import httpx from pipeline.db import get_db ODDS_API_KEY = os.environ.get("ODDS_API_KEY", "") if not ODDS_API_KEY: return {"error": "ODDS_API_KEY not set in Railway environment variables"} SPORT = "americanfootball_ncaaf" BASE_URL = "https://api.the-odds-api.com/v4" # Friday evening + Saturday morning snapshots for each week SNAPSHOTS = { 2025: { 1: ("2025-08-29T20:00:00Z", "2025-08-30T12:00:00Z"), 2: ("2025-09-05T20:00:00Z", "2025-09-06T12:00:00Z"), 3: ("2025-09-12T20:00:00Z", "2025-09-13T12:00:00Z"), 4: ("2025-09-19T20:00:00Z", ("2025-10-17T20:00:00Z", "2025-10-18T12:00:00Z"), 9: ("2025-10-24T20:00:00Z", "2025-10-25T12:00:00Z"), 10: ("2025-10-31T20:00:00Z", "2025-11-01T12:00:00Z"), 11: ("2025-11-07T20:00:00Z", week: int = 2): """ Shows the top 10 POTW candidates for a given week with their scores. Use this to diagnose why certain weeks have no POTW pick. """ try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, home_moneyline, away_moneyline, provider, opening_spread, opening_over_under, opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) PROVIDER_PRIORITY = ["Bovada", "the-odds-api", "consensus", "ESPN Bet", "DraftKings", "FanDuel"] lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") provider = r.get("provider", "") for key in [(ht, at, s, w), (ht, at, s, None)]: existing = lines.get(key) if existing is None: lines[key] = r else: ep = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == existing.get("provider","")), 99) np = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == provider), 99) if np < ep: lines[key] = r week_games_all = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("season") == season and g.get("week") == week] week_games = [g for g in week_games_all if g.get("home_points") is not lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: no_line.append(f"{ht} vs {at}") continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue mkt = ol["spread"] ens = r["ensemble_spread"] edge = abs(ens - mkt) if mkt is not None else 0 candidates.append({ "game": f"{ht} vs {at}", "spread_tier": r["spread_tier"], "edge": round(edge, 1), "agreement": r.get("spread_agreement"), "ensemble": round(ens, 1) if ens else None, "market": mkt, "provider": line.get("provider"), }) candidates.sort(key=lambda x: ( {"A+": 3, "A": 2, "B": 1, "C": 0}.get(x["spread_tier"], 0), x["edge"] ), reverse=True) return { "season": season, "week": week, "total_games_in_db": len(week_games_all), "completed_games": len(week_games), "games_no_line": len(no_line), "no_line_games": no_line[:10], "top_candidates": candidates[:10], "sample_games": [f"{g['home_team']} vs {g['away_team']} (pts: {g.get('home_points')}/{g.get('away_points')})" for g in week_games_all[:5]], } except Exception as e: import traceback return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/odds/backfill-opening-lines") def backfill_opening_lines(season: int = 2025): """ Pulls historical OPENING lines from The Odds API for an entire season and updates betting_lines table with opening_spread, opening_over_under, opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml, and calculates spread_movement. The Odds API historical endpoint format: GET /v4/historical/sports/americanfootball_ncaaf/odds ?apiKey=...&date=®ions=us&markets=spreads,totals,h2h We hit the earliest available timestamp for each week (typically Tuesday after the previous week's games) to get opening lines. """ import traceback import os import requests from datetime import datetime, timedelta try: from pipeline.db import get_db from models.adjustments import build_games_index ODDS_API_KEY = os.environ.get("ODDS_API_KEY", "") if not ODDS_API_KEY: return {"error": "ODDS_API_KEY not set in environment"} db = get_db() # Get all games for the season games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("start_date", "null") ) if not games_raw: return {"error": f"No games found for season {season}"} def norm(s): import re # Strip common team nicknames that appear in Odds API but not CFBD nicknames = [ "wildcats", "buckeyes", "tigers", "bulldogs", "eagles", "bears", "wolverines", "nittany lions", "mountaineers", "aggies", "longhorns", "crimson tide", "gators", "seminoles", "hurricanes", "volunteers", "razorbacks", "rebels", "war eagle", "auburn", "gamecocks", "tar heels", "wolfpack", "blue devils", "demon deacons", "yellow jackets", "hokies", "cavaliers", "scarlet knights", "cornhuskers", "hawkeyes", "badgers", "golden gophers", "fighting illini", "boilermakers", "hoosiers", "spartans", "fighting irish", "sooners", "cowboys", "jayhawks", "horned frogs", "mustangs", "bears", "cyclones", "cougars", "utes", "falcons", "rams", "trojans", "bruins", "ducks", "beavers", "huskies", "sun devils", "wildcats", "lobos", "aztecs", "rainbow warriors", "wolf pack", "broncos", "cowboys", "air force", "navy midshipmen", "army black knights", "midshipmen", "black knights", "golden knights", "rebels", "running rebels", "mean green", "red raiders", "panthers", "cardinals", "pirates", "knights", "owls", "flames", "hilltoppers", "toppers", "golden flashes", "zips", "chippewas", "broncos", "falcons", "rockets", "redhawks", "cardinals", "penguins", "bobcats", "chanticleers", "jaguars", "thundering herd", "golden eagles", "monarchs", "seahawks", "dukes", "spiders", "retrievers", "terrapins", "terps", "razorbacks", "warhawks", "ragin cajuns", "red wolves", "bearkats", "roadrunners", "miners", "49ers", "chargers", "flash", "panthers", "nittany", ] s = s.lower().strip() s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9 ]", "", s) # Remove nickname suffixes for nick in sorted(nicknames, key=len, reverse=True): if s.endswith(" " + nick): s = s[: -(len(nick) + 1)].strip() break replacements = { "state": "st", "university": "", "college": "", } for old_w, new_w in replacements.items(): s = s.replace(old_w, new_w) return re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip() # Build game index by normalized names cfbd_index = {} for g in games_raw: hk = norm(g["home_team"]) ak = norm(g["away_team"]) cfbd_index[(hk, ak)] = g # Group games by week to determine what date to query from collections import defaultdict weeks_games = defaultdict(list) for g in games_raw: weeks_games[g["week"]].append(g) total_updated = 0 week_results = [] for week in sorted(weeks_games.keys()): wk_games = weeks_games[week] # Find the earliest game date in this week dates = [] for g in wk_games: try: dt = datetime.fromisoformat(g["start_date"].replace("Z", "+00:00")) dates.append(dt) except: pass if not dates: continue earliest = min(dates) # Query 7 days before the first game to get opening lines # Opening lines typically posted Tuesday-Thursday before game week query_date = (earliest - timedelta(days=7)).strftime("%Y-%m-%dT12:00:00Z") url = "https://api.the-odds-api.com/v4/historical/sports/americanfootball_ncaaf/odds" params = { "apiKey": ODDS_API_KEY, "date": query_date, "regions": "us", "markets": "spreads,totals,h2h", "oddsFormat": "american", } try: resp = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=30) if resp.status_code != 200: week_results.append({"week": week, "error": f"HTTP {resp.status_code}", "updated": 0}) continue data = resp.json() games_data = data.get("data", []) except Exception as e: week_results.append({"week": week, "error": str(e), "updated": 0}) continue # Build map from API response game_map = {} for g in games_data: ht = g.get("home_team", "") at = g.get("away_team", "") hk = norm(ht) ak = norm(at) game_map[(hk, ak)] = g updated = 0 unmatched = [] for (hk, ak), raw in game_map.items(): cfbd = cfbd_index.get((hk, ak)) if cfbd is None: unmatched.append(f"{raw.get('away_team')} @ {raw.get('home_team')}") continue # Parse opening odds opening_spread = opening_ou = opening_home_ml = opening_away_ml = None bm_priority = ["bovada", "draftkings", "fanduel", "betmgm"] chosen = None for bk in bm_priority: for b in raw.get("bookmakers", []): if b.get("key") == bk: chosen = b break if chosen: break if not chosen and raw.get("bookmakers"): chosen = raw["bookmakers"][0] if chosen: for mkt in chosen.get("markets", []): mk = mkt.get("key") outs = mkt.get("outcomes", []) if mk == "spreads": for o in outs: if norm(o.get("name", "")).lower() == hk: opening_spread = o.get("point") elif mk == "totals": for o in outs: if o.get("name") == "Over": opening_ou = o.get("point") elif mk == "h2h": for o in outs: n = norm(o.get("name", "")).lower() if n == hk: opening_home_ml = o.get("price") elif n == ak: opening_away_ml = o.get("price") if opening_spread is None and opening_ou is None: continue # Get current closing line to calculate movement existing = db.table("betting_lines") \ .select("spread, over_under") \ .eq("home_team", cfbd["home_team"]) \ .eq("away_team", cfbd["away_team"]) \ .eq("season", season) \ .eq("week", cfbd["week"]) \ .execute() closing_spread = closing_ou = None if existing.data: closing_spread = existing.data[0].get("spread") closing_ou = existing.data[0].get("over_under") spread_movement = None ou_movement = None if opening_spread is not None and closing_spread is not None: spread_movement = round(closing_spread - opening_spread, 1) if opening_ou is not None and closing_ou is not None: ou_movement = round(closing_ou - opening_ou, 1) # Update the existing record try: db.table("betting_lines") \ .update({ "opening_spread": opening_spread, "opening_over_under": opening_ou, "opening_home_ml": opening_home_ml, "opening_away_ml": opening_away_ml, "spread_movement": spread_movement, "ou_movement": ou_movement, }) \ .eq("home_team", cfbd["home_team"]) \ .eq("away_team", cfbd["away_team"]) \ .eq("season", season) \ .eq("week", cfbd["week"]) \ .execute() updated += 1 total_updated += 1 except Exception as e: pass week_results.append({ "week": week, "queried_date": query_date, "games_from_api": len(game_map), "updated": updated, "unmatched_sample": unmatched[:3], }) return { "season": season, "total_updated": total_updated, "weeks": week_results, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/backtest/sharp-money-analysis") def sharp_money_analysis(season: int = 2025): """ Analyzes performance when sharp money agrees vs disagrees with model picks. Uses line movement (closing - opening) as a proxy for sharp money direction. Sharp agrees = line moved in same direction as model pick Sharp disagrees = line moved against model pick No movement = line didn't move or no opening line data """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db BET = 100 def pnl_spread(hit): if hit is None: return 0 return round(BET * 100/110, 2) if hit else -BET all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, start_date, home_points, away_points") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_points", "null") ) games_idx = build_games_index(fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, start_date, home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) )) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, home_moneyline, away_moneyline, provider, opening_spread, spread_movement") .not_.is_("home_team", "null") .eq("season", season) ) PROVIDER_PRIORITY = ["Bovada", "the-odds-api", "consensus", "ESPN Bet", "DraftKings", "FanDuel"] lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() key = (ht, at, season, r.get("week")) existing = lines.get(key) if existing is None: lines[key] = r else: ep = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == existing.get("provider","")), 99) np = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == r.get("provider","")), 99) if np < ep: lines[key] = r # Buckets: sharp_agree, sharp_disagree, no_data buckets = { "sharp_agree": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0, "pnl": 0}, "sharp_disagree": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0, "pnl": 0}, "no_data": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0, "pnl": 0}, } # Also track by movement magnitude by_magnitude = { "0.0-0.5": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0}, "0.5-1.0": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0}, "1.0-2.0": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0}, "2.0+": {"bets": 0, "hits": 0}, } for game in all_games_raw: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) week = game["week"] ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) if not line or not line.get("spread"): continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue if r.get("spread_tier") not in ("A+", "A"): continue mkt_spread = ol["spread"] actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) ens_spread = r.get("ensemble_spread") if ens_spread is None: continue # Determine hit pick_home = ens_spread < mkt_spread push = actual_margin == -mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = None if push else (home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered) pnl = pnl_spread(hit) # Sharp signal spread_movement = line.get("spread_movement") if spread_movement is not None and abs(spread_movement) >= 0.25: sharp_pick_home = spread_movement < 0 agrees = (pick_home == sharp_pick_home) bucket = "sharp_agree" if agrees else "sharp_disagree" mag = abs(spread_movement) if mag < 0.5: mag_key = "0.0-0.5" elif mag < 1.0: mag_key = "0.5-1.0" elif mag < 2.0: mag_key = "1.0-2.0" else: mag_key = "2.0+" by_magnitude[mag_key]["bets"] += 1 if hit: by_magnitude[mag_key]["hits"] += 1 else: bucket = "no_data" buckets[bucket]["bets"] += 1 if hit: buckets[bucket]["hits"] += 1 buckets[bucket]["pnl"] = round(buckets[bucket]["pnl"] + pnl, 2) # Calculate hit rates results = {} for k, v in buckets.items(): b = v["bets"] h = v["hits"] results[k] = { "bets": b, "hits": h, "hit_pct": round(h/b*100, 1) if b else 0, "pnl": v["pnl"], "roi": round(v["pnl"]/(b*BET)*100, 1) if b else 0, } mag_results = {} for k, v in by_magnitude.items(): b = v["bets"] h = v["hits"] mag_results[k] = { "bets": b, "hits": h, "hit_pct": round(h/b*100, 1) if b else 0, } return { "season": season, "summary": results, "by_movement_magnitude": mag_results, "interpretation": { "sharp_agree": "Model pick + line moved same direction = sharp money confirms", "sharp_disagree": "Model pick + line moved opposite direction = sharp money fades", "no_data": "No opening line or movement < 0.25 pts", } } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/backtest/sharp-potw") def sharp_potw_backtest(season: int = 2025, min_movement: float = 2.0): """ Sharp Money Pick of the Week backtest. Each week selects the single best A+ pick where: - Line moved >= min_movement points in same direction as model pick - Highest composite score wins Uses $250 flat bet at actual odds. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine from pipeline.db import get_db BET_SIZE = 250 def potw_score(r, game): base = 0.0 tier = r.get("spread_tier", "C") if tier == "A+": base += 50.0 elif tier == "A": base += 30.0 base += min(20.0, (r.get("edge_spread") or 0) * 2) base += (r.get("spread_agreement") or 0) * 5.0 return base all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, start_date, home_points, away_points") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("home_points", "null") ) games_idx = build_games_index(fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, neutral_site, start_date, home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) )) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, home_moneyline, away_moneyline, provider, opening_spread, opening_over_under, opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml, spread_movement, ou_movement") .not_.is_("home_team", "null") .eq("season", season) ) PROVIDER_PRIORITY = ["Bovada", "the-odds-api", "consensus", "ESPN Bet", "DraftKings", "FanDuel"] lines = {} for ln in lines_raw: ht = (ln.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (ln.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() key = (ht, at, season, ln.get("week")) existing = lines.get(key) if existing is None: lines[key] = ln else: ep = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == existing.get("provider","")), 99) np = next((i for i, p in enumerate(PROVIDER_PRIORITY) if p == ln.get("provider","")), 99) if np < ep: lines[key] = ln from collections import defaultdict games_by_week = defaultdict(list) for g in all_games_raw: games_by_week[g["week"]].append(g) cumulative_pnl = 0 wins = losses = 0 sharp_potw_weeks = [] for week in sorted(games_by_week.keys()): candidates = [] for game in games_by_week[week]: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) if not line or not line.get("spread"): continue spread_movement = line.get("spread_movement") if spread_movement is None or abs(spread_movement) < min_movement: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season-1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season-1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) ol = get_opening_line(line) r = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp, elo, ppa, advanced, ol["spread"], ol["over_under"], ol["home_moneyline"], ol["away_moneyline"], adj=adj) if not r: continue if r.get("spread_tier") != "A+": continue # A+ only for Sharp POTW edge = r.get("edge_spread") or 0 agr = r.get("spread_agreement") or 0 if edge > 15: continue # cap extreme edges — noise not signal if agr < 3: continue # require at least 3 models to agree mkt_spread = line["spread"] ens_spread = r.get("ensemble_spread") if ens_spread is None: continue # Check sharp money agrees with model model_pick_home = ens_spread < mkt_spread sharp_pick_home = spread_movement < 0 # negative = moved toward home if model_pick_home != sharp_pick_home: continue # sharp disagrees, skip score = potw_score(r, game) # Bonus for larger movement score += min(10.0, abs(spread_movement) * 2) candidates.append((score, r, game, line, spread_movement)) if not candidates: continue candidates.sort(key=lambda x: -x[0]) score, r, game, line, spread_movement = candidates[0] ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] mkt_spread = line["spread"] actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) ens_spread = r["ensemble_spread"] pick_home = ens_spread < mkt_spread push = actual_margin == -mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = None if push else (home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered) if hit is None: pnl = 0 elif hit: pnl = round(BET_SIZE * 100/110, 2) else: pnl = -BET_SIZE cumulative_pnl += pnl if hit is None: pass elif hit: wins += 1 else: losses += 1 pick_team = ht if pick_home else at home_is_fav = mkt_spread < 0 abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) if pick_home: pick_display = f"{pick_team} {f'-{abs_spread}' if home_is_fav else f'+{abs_spread}'}" else: pick_display = f"{pick_team} {f'+{abs_spread}' if home_is_fav else f'-{abs_spread}'}" sharp_potw_weeks.append({ "week": week, "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pick": pick_display, "spread_tier": r["spread_tier"], "composite_score": round(score, 2), "ensemble_spread": round(ens_spread, 1), "market_spread": mkt_spread, "opening_spread": line.get("opening_spread"), "spread_movement": round(spread_movement, 1), "edge": round(r.get("edge_spread") or 0, 1), "agreement": r.get("spread_agreement"), "actual_margin": actual_margin, "hit": hit, "pnl": pnl, "cumulative_pnl": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "bankroll": round(BET_SIZE + cumulative_pnl, 2), }) total = wins + losses return { "season": season, "min_movement": min_movement, "bet_size": BET_SIZE, "starting_bankroll": BET_SIZE, "final_bankroll": round(BET_SIZE + cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_profit": round(cumulative_pnl, 2), "total_weeks": len(sharp_potw_weeks), "wins": wins, "losses": losses, "hit_pct": round(wins/total*100, 1) if total else 0, "roi": round(cumulative_pnl/BET_SIZE*100, 1), "weeks": sharp_potw_weeks, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/odds/snapshot") def snapshot_current_lines(): """ Saves a snapshot of current live lines with timestamp. Run this Wednesday/Thursday to capture mid-week lines for sharp money calculation. Stores in line_snapshots table: home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, timestamp. """ import traceback import os import requests from datetime import datetime, timezone try: from pipeline.db import get_db import re ODDS_API_KEY = os.environ.get("ODDS_API_KEY", "") if not ODDS_API_KEY: return {"error": "ODDS_API_KEY not set"} db = get_db() # Get current season and week from games table from datetime import datetime, timezone now = datetime.now(timezone.utc) upcoming = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("season, week, home_team, away_team, start_date") .gte("start_date", now.isoformat()) .order("start_date") .limit(200) ) if not upcoming: return {"error": "No upcoming games found"} season = upcoming[0]["season"] week = upcoming[0]["week"] # Fetch current lines from Odds API url = "https://api.the-odds-api.com/v4/sports/americanfootball_ncaaf/odds" params = { "apiKey": ODDS_API_KEY, "regions": "us", "markets": "spreads,totals,h2h", "oddsFormat": "american", } resp = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=30) if resp.status_code != 200: return {"error": f"Odds API returned {resp.status_code}"} games_data = resp.json() def norm(s): s = s.lower().strip() s = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9 ]", "", s) nicknames = ["wildcats","buckeyes","tigers","bulldogs","eagles","bears", "wolverines","nittany lions","mountaineers","aggies","longhorns", "crimson tide","gators","seminoles","hurricanes","volunteers", "razorbacks","rebels","gamecocks","tar heels","wolfpack", "blue devils","demon deacons","yellow jackets","hokies", "cavaliers","scarlet knights","cornhuskers","hawkeyes","badgers", "golden gophers","fighting illini","boilermakers","hoosiers", "spartans","fighting irish","sooners","cowboys","jayhawks", "horned frogs","mustangs","cyclones","cougars","utes","falcons", "rams","trojans","bruins","ducks","beavers","huskies","sun devils", "lobos","aztecs","rainbow warriors","wolf pack","broncos", "mean green","red raiders","panthers","cardinals","pirates", "knights","owls","flames","hilltoppers","golden flashes","zips", "chippewas","rockets","redhawks","penguins","bobcats","chanticleers", "jaguars","thundering herd","golden eagles","monarchs","dukes", "warhawks","ragin cajuns","red wolves","bearkats","roadrunners", "miners","midshipmen","black knights"] for nick in sorted(nicknames, key=len, reverse=True): if s.endswith(" " + nick): s = s[:-(len(nick)+1)].strip() break s = s.replace("state","st").replace("university","").replace("college","") return re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s).strip() # Build game lookup from DB game_lookup = {} for g in upcoming: hk = norm(g["home_team"]) ak = norm(g["away_team"]) game_lookup[(hk, ak)] = g snapshot_time = now.isoformat() inserted = 0 unmatched = [] for g in games_data: ht_api = g.get("home_team", "") at_api = g.get("away_team", "") hk = norm(ht_api) ak = norm(at_api) cfbd = game_lookup.get((hk, ak)) if not cfbd: unmatched.append(f"{at_api} @ {ht_api}") continue # Parse current spread and total current_spread = current_total = None bm_priority = ["bovada", "draftkings", "fanduel", "betmgm"] chosen = None for bk in bm_priority: for b in g.get("bookmakers", []): if b.get("key") == bk: chosen = b break if chosen: break if not chosen and g.get("bookmakers"): chosen = g["bookmakers"][0] if chosen: for mkt in chosen.get("markets", []): mk = mkt.get("key") if mk == "spreads": for o in mkt.get("outcomes", []): if norm(o.get("name","")) == hk: current_spread = o.get("point") elif mk == "totals": for o in mkt.get("outcomes", []): if o.get("name") == "Over": current_total = o.get("point") if current_spread is None: continue try: db.table("line_snapshots").insert({ "home_team": cfbd["home_team"], "away_team": cfbd["away_team"], "season": season, "week": week, "spread": current_spread, "over_under": current_total, "snapshot_time": snapshot_time, }).execute() inserted += 1 except Exception as e: pass return { "snapshot_time": snapshot_time, "season": season, "week": week, "inserted": inserted, "unmatched_sample": unmatched[:5], } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/tier-distribution") def tier_distribution(season: int = 2025, week: int = 1): """ Shows how many picks qualify at each tier threshold for a given week.
