Plain-English projection if ens_margin is not None: if ens_margin > 0: model_winner = ht model_loser = at else: model_winner = at model_loser = ht projection_summary = f"Model expects {model_winner} to win by {abs(ens_margin):.1f}." else: projection_summary = "No projection available." # What the spread pick means in plain English if spread_pick and mkt_spread is not None and ens_margin is not None: spread_pick_line_num = -mkt_spread if spread_pick == ht else mkt_spread spread_pick_line_str = f"{spread_pick} {spread_pick_line_num:+g}" if spread_pick == market_fav_team: spread_pick_summary = f"Model picks the favorite ({spread_pick_line_str}) — has more confidence in {spread_pick} than the market does." else: spread_pick_summary = f"Model picks the underdog ({spread_pick_line_str}) — thinks the market is overrating {market_fav_team}." else: spread_pick_summary = "No spread pick." # Total pick in plain English if ou_pick and mkt_total is not None and ens_total is not None: total_pick_summary = f"Model projects total of {ens_total:.1f} vs market {mkt_total} — picks the {ou_pick.upper()}." else: total_pick_summary = "No total pick." # ML pick in plain English if ml_pick: ml_team = ht if ml_pick == "home" else at ml_price = home_ml if ml_pick == "home" else away_ml ml_pick_summary = f"Model likes {ml_team} ML at {ml_price:+g}." if ml_price is not None else f"Model likes {ml_team} ML." else: ml_pick_summary = "No moneyline pick." home_players = players_blurb(ht) away_players = players_blurb(at) # ── PRE-GAME PROMPT ── pre_prompt = f"""You are an analytical writer for PressBox Analytics, a college football betting analysis site. Write a SHARP, specific, 4-5 sentence pre-game blurb for this matchup. YOUR VOICE: - Analytical, not emotional. No hype words ("massive", "explosive matchup", "epic"). - Cite specific players by name when they're relevant to what the model sees. - If the model has a strong opinion, say what it is and WHY (pace, defensive matchup, etc.). - If no edge, say so plainly — don't fabricate analysis. - Never use phrases like "our model", "the algorithm", "AI predicts". Just describe what's true. - Never reveal specific weights, thresholds, or that this is SP+-based. MATCHUP: {at} (away) at {ht} (home), Week {week} {season} MARKET LINE: {market_summary} Total: {mkt_total if mkt_total else 'N/A'} WHAT THE MODEL SEES: {projection_summary} Projected total: {f"{ens_total:.1f}" if ens_total else "N/A"} (market: {mkt_total or 'N/A'}) THE PICKS (use these EXACTLY — do not flip teams or directions): - SPREAD: {spread_pick_summary} (conviction: {tier_label(spread_tier)}) - TOTAL: {total_pick_summary} (conviction: {tier_label(ou_tier)}) - MONEYLINE: {ml_pick_summary} (conviction: {tier_label(ml_tier)}) EDGES: - Spread edge vs market: {f"{edge_spread:.1f} points" if edge_spread else "—"} - Total edge vs market: {f"{edge_total:.1f} points" if edge_total else "—"} PRODUCTS THIS WEEK: {products_str} SITUATIONAL NOTES: {", ".join(adj_notes) if adj_notes else "None flagged"} {ht.upper()} KEY RETURNING PRODUCTION (home): {home_players} {at.upper()} KEY RETURNING PRODUCTION (away): {away_players} Write a 4-5 sentence analytical pre-game blurb. - Open with what the model thinks of the matchup vs the market. - Reference at least one specific player by name if relevant. - End with which products fire for this game (POTW / TOTW / Smart Money / Lottery), or note that no headline product is in play. - CRITICAL: do not invert who is favored, who is home, or who the pick is. Use the picks exactly as stated above. Output only the blurb. No headers, no markdown.""" pre_blurb = call_claude(pre_prompt, max_tokens=500) # ── POST-GAME PROMPT ── post_blurb = None if has_result: home_pts = game["home_points"] away_pts = game["away_points"] actual_margin = game["actual_margin"] actual_total = game["actual_total"] spread_result = game.get("spread_result") ou_result_val = game.get("ou_result") ml_result_val = game.get("ml_result") post_prompt = f"""You are an analytical writer for PressBox Analytics. Write a SHARP, specific, 4-5 sentence post-game blurb that explains what happened relative to what the model projected. YOUR VOICE: - Specific. Cite the score, the spread margin, who covered, the total. - Honest. If the model was right, say briefly why it nailed it. If wrong, name why it missed (turnovers, weather, injury impact, etc.) — DO NOT just say "the model was wrong" without a reason. - Reference specific players if a standout performance drove the result. - No emotional language. No "shocker", "stunner", "blew the doors off". Just describe what occurred. - Don't mention specific model names, weights, or that this is SP+-based. MATCHUP: {at} (away) at {ht} (home), Week {week} {season} MARKET LINE (pre-game): {market_summary} FINAL SCORE: {ht} {home_pts}, {at} {away_pts} Actual margin: {ht} {'won by' if actual_margin > 0 else 'lost by'} {abs(actual_margin)} Actual total: {actual_total} WHAT THE MODEL PROJECTED: {projection_summary} Projected total: {f"{ens_total:.1f}" if ens_total else "N/A"} (actual: {actual_total}) THE PICKS AND HOW THEY GRADED (use teams EXACTLY as stated): - SPREAD: {spread_pick_summary} → result: {spread_result or 'no pick'} ({tier_label(spread_tier)}) - TOTAL: {total_pick_summary} → result: {ou_result_val or 'no pick'} ({tier_label(ou_tier)}) - ML: {ml_pick_summary} → result: {ml_result_val or 'no pick'} ({tier_label(ml_tier)}) {ht.upper()} KEY PLAYERS (home): {home_players} {at.upper()} KEY PLAYERS (away): {away_players} Write 4-5 sentences. - Lead with what actually happened (final score, who covered the spread, total result). - Compare to the projection — note magnitude of the miss or hit. - Cite at least one player's role in the outcome if relevant. - Close with how the headline products (POTW / TOTW / Smart Money / Lottery) fared if any fired. - CRITICAL: do not invert who was favored, who covered, or who the pick was. Use the picks and teams exactly as stated above. Output only the blurb. No headers, no markdown.""" post_blurb = call_claude(post_prompt, max_tokens=500) db.table("game_narratives").upsert({ "game_id": game_id, "season": season, "week": week, "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "pre_game_blurb": pre_blurb, "post_game_blurb": post_blurb, }, on_conflict="game_id").execute() generated += 1 time.sleep(0.2) next_offset = offset + limit return { "season": season, "week": week, "generated": generated, "skipped": skipped, "batch": len(games), "total_games": total, "next_offset": next_offset if next_offset < total else None, "done": next_offset >= total, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/inspect-matchup") def inspect_matchup(team1: str, team2: str, season: int = 2025): """ Returns every row in every table touching a given matchup. Use this when 'duplicates' appear on the games page so we can see which table is actually duplicated. Usage: /admin/inspect-matchup?team1=Georgia Southern&team2=Fresno State&season=2025 """ import traceback try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() # Games rows games_t1_home = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, home_points, away_points, season_type") .eq("home_team", team1).eq("away_team", team2).eq("season", season) ) games_t2_home = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, home_points, away_points, season_type") .eq("home_team", team2).eq("away_team", team1).eq("season", season) ) # Narratives try: narr_rows = fetch_all( db.table("game_narratives") .select("game_id, season, week, home_team, away_team, " "pre_game_blurb, post_game_blurb") .eq("season", season) .in_("home_team", [team1, team2]) .in_("away_team", [team1, team2]) ) except Exception as e: narr_rows = [{"error": str(e)}] # Betting lines try: lines_rows = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, provider") .eq("season", season) .in_("home_team", [team1, team2]) .in_("away_team", [team1, team2]) ) except Exception as e: lines_rows = [{"error": str(e)}] return { "season": season, "team1": team1, "team2": team2, "games_rows_count": len(games_t1_home) + len(games_t2_home), "games_rows": games_t1_home + games_t2_home, "narrative_rows_count": len(narr_rows), "narrative_rows": [ {k: v for k, v in r.items() if k not in ("pre_game_blurb", "post_game_blurb")} for r in narr_rows ], "betting_lines_count": len(lines_rows), "betting_lines": lines_rows, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/dedupe-games") def dedupe_games(season: int = None, dry_run: bool = True): """ Find and delete duplicate game rows from the `games` table. Matchup keys are orderless: (sorted(home, away), season). This catches both: - Exact dupes (same teams, same week) - Swapped dupes (home/away inverted) - Same-season dupes in different week labels Keeps the row with scores; if multiple have scores, keeps the lowest id. Usage: /admin/dedupe-games?season=2025&dry_run=true ← preview only /admin/dedupe-games?season=2025&dry_run=false ← actually delete """ import traceback try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() q = db.table("games").select( "id, home_team, away_team, season, week, home_points, away_points" ) if season is not None: q = q.eq("season", season) rows = fetch_all(q) from collections import defaultdict groups = defaultdict(list) for r in rows: # Orderless team key so home/away swaps collapse to same group. # Same season required; week NOT required (catches "Week 0" vs "Week 1"). teams_sorted = tuple(sorted([r.get("home_team") or "", r.get("away_team") or ""])) key = (teams_sorted, r.get("season")) groups[key].append(r) to_delete = [] kept_examples = [] for key, dupes in groups.items(): if len(dupes) < 2: continue def sort_key(r): has_score = (r.get("home_points") is not None and r.get("away_points") is not None) return (0 if has_score else 1, r.get("id")) dupes_sorted = sorted(dupes, key=sort_key) keeper = dupes_sorted[0] dupes_to_remove = dupes_sorted[1:] for d in dupes_to_remove: to_delete.append(d["id"]) if len(kept_examples) < 20: kept_examples.append({ "teams": list(key[0]), "season": key[1], "kept": { "id": keeper["id"], "home": keeper["home_team"], "away": keeper["away_team"], "week": keeper["week"], "has_score": keeper.get("home_points") is not None, "score": (f"{keeper['home_team']} {keeper['home_points']}, " f"{keeper['away_team']} {keeper['away_points']}") if keeper.get("home_points") is not None else None, }, "deleted": [{ "id": d["id"], "home": d["home_team"], "away": d["away_team"], "week": d["week"], "has_score": d.get("home_points") is not None, } for d in dupes_to_remove], }) result = { "season": season, "dry_run": dry_run, "total_rows": len(rows), "duplicate_sets": sum(1 for dupes in groups.values() if len(dupes) > 1), "rows_to_delete": len(to_delete), "examples": kept_examples, } if not dry_run and to_delete: deleted = 0 BATCH = 100 for i in range(0, len(to_delete), BATCH): chunk = to_delete[i:i+BATCH] db.table("games").delete().in_("id", chunk).execute() deleted += len(chunk) result["actually_deleted"] = deleted return result except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/narrative-context-preview") def narrative_context_preview(season: int = 2025, week: int = 1, game_idx: int = 0): """ Returns the EXACT player context that will be injected into the narrative prompt for a single game. Use this to verify player loading is working before paying to regenerate. Usage: /admin/narrative-context-preview?season=2025&week=1&game_idx=0 """ import traceback try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() games_data = games_by_week(season=season, week=week) games = games_data.get("games", []) if not games: return {"error": "no games"} if game_idx >= len(games): return {"error": f"game_idx out of range (have {len(games)})"} game = games[game_idx] ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] # Replicate the player-loading logic from generate_narratives team_players = {} # Skill skill_rows = fetch_all( db.table("player_seasons") .select("player_id, team, position, player_value, ppa_total_all, " "ppa_total_pass, ppa_total_rush, usage_overall") .eq("season", season) .in_("team", [ht, at]) .in_("position", ["QB", "RB", "WR", "TE", "HB"]) .not_.is_("player_value", "null") .order("player_value", desc=True) ) skill_pids = list({r["player_id"] for r in skill_rows if r.get("player_id")}) names_by_pid = {} for i in range(0, len(skill_pids), 500): chunk = skill_pids[i:i+500] name_rows = (db.table("players") .select("player_id, first_name, last_name") .in_("player_id", chunk).execute().data) or [] for nr in name_rows: names_by_pid[nr["player_id"]] = ( f"{(nr.get('first_name') or '').strip()} " f"{(nr.get('last_name') or '').strip()}").strip() for r in skill_rows: t = r.get("team") if t not in team_players: team_players[t] = [] sc = sum(1 for p in team_players[t] if p["pos"] in ("QB","RB","WR","TE","HB")) if sc >= 3: continue pid = r.get("player_id") name = names_by_pid.get(pid) if not name: continue team_players[t].append({ "name": name, "pos": r.get("position", ""), "player_value": r.get("player_value"), }) # Defense def_rows = fetch_all( db.table("player_stats") .select("player_id, team, position, sacks, tackles_for_loss, " "tackles, def_interceptions, passes_broken_up") .eq("season", season) .in_("team", [ht, at]) .in_("position", ["DL", "DE", "DT", "EDGE", "LB", "ILB", "OLB", "DB", "CB", "S", "FS", "SS"]) ) # Lookup defender names from players table def_pids = list({r["player_id"] for r in def_rows if r.get("player_id")}) def_names_by_pid = {} for i in range(0, len(def_pids), 500): chunk = def_pids[i:i+500] name_rows = (db.table("players") .select("player_id, first_name, last_name") .in_("player_id", chunk).execute().data) or [] for nr in name_rows: def_names_by_pid[nr["player_id"]] = ( f"{(nr.get('first_name') or '').strip()} " f"{(nr.get('last_name') or '').strip()}").strip() for r in def_rows: r["_impact"] = ( (r.get("sacks") or 0) * 3 + (r.get("tackles_for_loss") or 0) * 2 + (r.get("def_interceptions") or 0) * 4 + (r.get("passes_broken_up") or 0) * 1 + (r.get("tackles") or 0) * 0.1 ) def_by_team = {} for r in def_rows: def_by_team.setdefault(r["team"], []).append(r) for t, defs in def_by_team.items(): defs.sort(key=lambda x: -x["_impact"]) if t not in team_players: team_players[t] = [] for r in defs[:2]: name = def_names_by_pid.get(r.get("player_id")) if not name: continue team_players[t].append({ "name": name, "pos": r.get("position", ""), "impact": round(r["_impact"], 1), }) return { "season": season, "week": week, "game": f"{at} @ {ht}", "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "home_players": team_players.get(ht, []), "away_players": team_players.get(at, []), "home_count": len(team_players.get(ht, [])), "away_count": len(team_players.get(at, [])), } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/regen-narratives-season") def regen_narratives_season(season: int = 2025, start_week: int = 1, end_week: int = 16, batch_size: int = 10, overwrite: bool = True): """ Regenerate narratives for ALL games in a season under the new tier system. Processes one week at a time, looping until done. Designed for one-shot use after a tier/model change. Usage: /admin/regen-narratives-season?season=2025 /admin/regen-narratives-season?season=2025&overwrite=true /admin/regen-narratives-season?season=2025&start_week=8&end_week=15 """ import traceback try: results = [] total_generated = 0 total_skipped = 0 for week in range(start_week, end_week + 1): week_offset = 0 week_generated = 0 week_skipped = 0 while True: r = generate_narratives(season=season, week=week, overwrite=overwrite, limit=batch_size, offset=week_offset) if "error" in r: results.append({"week": week, "offset": week_offset, "error": r["error"]}) break week_generated += r.get("generated", 0) week_skipped += r.get("skipped", 0) if r.get("done"): break week_offset = r.get("next_offset", week_offset + batch_size) if week_offset is None: break results.append({ "week": week, "generated": week_generated, "skipped": week_skipped, "total": week_generated + week_skipped, }) total_generated += week_generated total_skipped += week_skipped return { "season": season, "weeks_processed": end_week - start_week + 1, "total_generated": total_generated, "total_skipped": total_skipped, "per_week": results, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} def call_claude(prompt: str, max_tokens: int = 500) -> str: """Call Claude API and return text response.""" import requests, os try: api_key = os.environ.get("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", "") resp = requests.post( "https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", headers={ "Content-Type": "application/json", "anthropic-version": "2023-06-01", "x-api-key": api_key, }, json={ "model": "claude-sonnet-4-5", "max_tokens": max_tokens, "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}], }, timeout=20, ) data = resp.json() if "content" in data and len(data["content"]) > 0: return data["content"][0]["text"].strip() elif "error" in data: return f"[API error: {data['error'].get('message', 'unknown')}]" else: return f"[Unexpected response: {str(data)[:100]}]" except Exception as e: return f"[Generation error: {str(e)}]" # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # FBS TEAM LIST # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── FBS_CONFERENCES = [ "ACC", "Big 12", "Big Ten", "SEC", "American Athletic", "Mountain West", "Sun Belt", "Conference USA", "Mid-American", "Pac-12", "FBS Independents" ] def get_fbs_teams(db, season: int = 2026) -> dict: """Returns dict of {team: conference} for FBS teams in given season.""" rows = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("home_team, home_conference") .eq("season", season) .in_("home_conference", FBS_CONFERENCES) ) return {r["home_team"]: r["home_conference"] for r in rows if r.get("home_team")} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # POWER RANKINGS ENDPOINT # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/rankings/power") def power_rankings(season: int = 2025, week: int = None, limit: int = 25): """ PressBox Rating — proprietary composite power ranking. The methodology blends multiple predictive signals weighted by their demonstrated value across four seasons of pick grading. Internal components and weights are intentionally not exposed in the response. Only FBS teams included. """ from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() fbs_teams = get_fbs_teams(db, 2026) phase = "preseason" if week is None else ( "early" if week <= 5 else "mid" if week <= 9 else "late" ) # ── SP+ (foundational signal) and ELO from team_ratings ── rating_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_ratings") .select("team, sp_overall, sp_offense, sp_defense, sp_special_teams, elo") .eq("season", season) ) team_data = {} for r in rating_rows: t = r.get("team") if not t or t not in fbs_teams: continue if t not in team_data: team_data[t] = { "team": t, "conference": fbs_teams[t], "sp_overall": None, "sp_offense": None, "sp_defense": None, "sp_special_teams": None, "elo": None, "ppa": None, "off_explosive": None, "def_explosive": None, "havoc": None, "off_success": None, "def_success": None, } if r.get("sp_overall") is not None: team_data[t]["sp_overall"] = r["sp_overall"] team_data[t]["sp_offense"] = r.get("sp_offense") team_data[t]["sp_defense"] = r.get("sp_defense") team_data[t]["sp_special_teams"] = r.get("sp_special_teams") if r.get("elo") is not None: team_data[t]["elo"] = r["elo"] # ── PPA season ── ppa_rows = fetch_all( db.table("ppa_season") .select("team, offense_overall, defense_overall") .eq("season", season) ) for r in ppa_rows: t = r.get("team") if t in team_data and r.get("offense_overall") is not None: off = r.get("offense_overall") or 0 def_ = r.get("defense_overall") or 0 team_data[t]["ppa"] = off - def_ # ── Advanced stats — havoc, explosiveness, success rates ── adv_rows = fetch_all( db.table("advanced_stats") .select("team, off_success_rate, def_success_rate, def_havoc_total, " "off_explosiveness, def_explosiveness") .eq("season", season) ) for r in adv_rows: t = r.get("team") if t in team_data: team_data[t]["off_success"] = r.get("off_success_rate") team_data[t]["def_success"] = r.get("def_success_rate") team_data[t]["havoc"] = r.get("def_havoc_total") team_data[t]["off_explosive"] = r.get("off_explosiveness") team_data[t]["def_explosive"] = r.get("def_explosiveness") # ── Roster movement adjustment ── # In the preseason (and early in the season) SP+ hasn't seen the new # roster yet — it's anchored on last year's team. So a team that lost # its star QB to the transfer portal still looks elite by SP+ alone. # We compute a per-team "roster delta" by summing the player_value of # players who LEFT vs. who ARRIVED. # Effect tapers off after Week 4 — by then SP+ has seen enough games. roster_delta = {} roster_delta_available = False if phase in ("preseason", "early"): try: # Pull all player_seasons rows for season-1 (last year, source team) # and season (where they are now). The "season" param to this endpoint # is typically 2025; "current" rosters live at season+1=2026. current_rows = fetch_all( db.table("player_seasons") .select("player_id, team") .eq("season", season + 1) ) current_team_by_pid = {r["player_id"]: r.get("team") for r in current_rows if r.get("player_id")} # CRITICAL: if we don't have any current-season roster data, DO NOT # apply the roster delta. Otherwise every player from last year would # appear "gone" and every team would get massive negative deltas. if current_team_by_pid: roster_delta_available = True prior_rows = fetch_all( db.table("player_seasons") .select("player_id, team, player_value") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("player_value", "null") ) prior_team_by_pid = {r["player_id"]: r.get("team") for r in prior_rows if r.get("player_id")} prior_value_by_pid = {r["player_id"]: r.get("player_value") for r in prior_rows if r.get("player_id")} for pid, prior_team in prior_team_by_pid.items(): pv = prior_value_by_pid.get(pid) if not prior_team or pv is None: continue current_team = current_team_by_pid.get(pid) if not current_team: # Player gone (graduated/NFL/cut) — prior team loses value roster_delta[prior_team] = roster_delta.get(prior_team, 0) - float(pv) elif current_team != prior_team: # Player transferred — prior team loses, new team gains roster_delta[prior_team] = roster_delta.get(prior_team, 0) - float(pv) roster_delta[current_team] = roster_delta.get(current_team, 0) + float(pv) # If current_team == prior_team: returner, no delta except Exception: roster_delta = {} roster_delta_available = False # ── Proprietary composite score ── # Weights intentionally not exposed via API. Tuned on 4-season pick grading. # Foundation is the strongest single signal; supporting components capture # what raw predictive models tend to underweight (havoc, explosiveness, # success-rate edges) plus a roster-movement adjustment that fires only in # preseason/early — by mid-season SP+ has caught up to the new roster. SP_W = 0.72 HAVOC_W = 0.10 EXPLO_W = 0.08 SUCCESS_W = 0.10 # Roster delta is a player_value sum; values range ±5-10 per player. # Scale so a single elite-QB loss (~6 player_value) ≈ -3 SP-equivalent pts. # In preseason this is at full weight; in early season it tapers. if phase == "preseason": ROSTER_W = 0.50 elif phase == "early": ROSTER_W = 0.25 else: ROSTER_W = 0.0 scored = [] for t, d in team_data.items(): sp = d["sp_overall"] if sp is None: continue # Without SP+ we can't anchor the composite # Normalize each supplemental component to an SP-equivalent point scale # (roughly ±20-pt range so the composite stays interpretable). havoc = d.get("havoc") or 0 # League average havoc ~16. Normalize centered at 16, scaled to ±10 pts. havoc_norm = (havoc - 16) * 0.6 off_exp = d.get("off_explosive") or 0 def_exp = d.get("def_explosive") or 0 # Explosiveness gap, scaled. explo_gap = off_exp - def_exp explo_norm = explo_gap * 12.0 off_sr = d.get("off_success") or 0 def_sr = d.get("def_success") or 0 success_gap = off_sr - def_sr success_norm = success_gap * 35.0 # Roster delta — sum of player_value of players gained minus lost rd = roster_delta.get(t, 0) # Composite — sum of weighted, normalized components. composite = ( sp * SP_W + havoc_norm * HAVOC_W + explo_norm * EXPLO_W + success_norm * SUCCESS_W + rd * ROSTER_W ) scored.append({ "team": t, "conference": d["conference"], "score": round(composite, 2), "sp_overall": sp, "sp_offense": d["sp_offense"], "sp_defense": d["sp_defense"], "sp_special_teams": d["sp_special_teams"], "elo": d["elo"], "ppa": round(d["ppa"], 4) if d["ppa"] is not None else None, }) scored.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True) conf_counters = {} ranked = [] for i, team in enumerate(scored): rank = i + 1 conf = team["conference"] conf_counters[conf] = conf_counters.get(conf, 0) + 1 ranked.append({**team, "rank": rank, "conference_rank": conf_counters[conf]}) return { "season": season, "week": week, "phase": phase, "basis": "PressBox Rating — proprietary composite", "total": len(ranked), "rankings": ranked[:limit], "full": ranked, "_debug_roster_delta_available": roster_delta_available, } # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # UPCOMING GAMES ENDPOINT # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/games/upcoming") def upcoming_games( season: int = 2026, week: int = None, conference: str = None, team: str = None, ): """ Returns upcoming games for a season with venue, date, ELO matchup data. Filters to FBS teams only. Optionally filter by week, conference, or team. """ from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() fbs_teams = get_fbs_teams(db, season) query = ( db.table("games") .select( "id, season, week, season_type, start_date, neutral_site, " "conference_game, home_team, home_conference, away_team, " "away_conference, venue, home_points, away_points, " "home_pregame_elo, away_pregame_elo" ) .eq("season", season) .eq("season_type", "regular") .in_("home_conference", FBS_CONFERENCES) ) if week is not None: query = query.eq("week", week) if conference: # Filter to games where either team is in the conference query = query.or_( f"home_conference.eq.{conference},away_conference.eq.{conference}" ) if team: query = query.or_( f"home_team.eq.{team},away_team.eq.{team}" ) rows = fetch_all(query.order("start_date")) # Filter to only include games where BOTH teams are FBS fbs_set = set(fbs_teams.keys()) games = [] for g in rows: ht = g.get("home_team", "") at = g.get("away_team", "") # Allow non-FBS away teams but flag them is_fbs_matchup = ht in fbs_set and at in fbs_set has_score = g.get("home_points") is not None # Format date raw_date = g.get("start_date", "") try: from datetime import datetime as _dt dt = _dt.fromisoformat(raw_date.replace("Z", "+00:00")) formatted_date = dt.strftime("%a, %b %d").replace(" 0", " ") formatted_time = dt.strftime("%I:%M %p ET").lstrip("0") if dt.hour != 4 else "TBD" except: formatted_date = raw_date[:10] if raw_date else "TBD" formatted_time = "TBD" games.append({ "game_id": str(g["id"]), "week": g.get("week"), "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "home_conference": g.get("home_conference"), "away_conference": g.get("away_conference"), "venue": g.get("venue"), "neutral_site": g.get("neutral_site", False), "conference_game": g.get("conference_game", False), "date": formatted_date, "time": formatted_time, "raw_date": raw_date, "home_elo": g.get("home_pregame_elo"), "away_elo": g.get("away_pregame_elo"), "has_score": has_score, "home_points": g.get("home_points"), "away_points": g.get("away_points"), "is_fbs_matchup": is_fbs_matchup, }) weeks = sorted(set(g["week"] for g in games if g["week"])) return { "season": season, "total": len(games), "weeks": weeks, "games": games, } # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # TEAMS ENDPOINT # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/teams") def teams_list(season: int = 2026): """ Returns all FBS teams grouped by conference with latest power ratings. """ from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() fbs_teams = get_fbs_teams(db, season) # Get power ratings for display (prior season) rating_season = season - 1 rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_ratings") .select("team, sp_overall, sp_offense, sp_defense, elo") .eq("season", rating_season) ) ratings = {} for r in rows: t = r.get("team") if not t: continue if t not in ratings: ratings[t] = {"sp_overall": None, "sp_offense": None, "sp_defense": None, "elo": None} if r.get("sp_overall") is not None: ratings[t]["sp_overall"] = r["sp_overall"] ratings[t]["sp_offense"] = r.get("sp_offense") ratings[t]["sp_defense"] = r.get("sp_defense") if r.get("elo") is not None: ratings[t]["elo"] = r["elo"] # Group by conference by_conf = {} for team, conf in sorted(fbs_teams.items()): if conf not in by_conf: by_conf[conf] = [] r = ratings.get(team, {}) by_conf[conf].append({ "team": team, "conference": conf, "sp_overall": r.get("sp_overall"), "sp_offense": r.get("sp_offense"), "sp_defense": r.get("sp_defense"), "elo": r.get("elo"), }) # Sort teams within each conference by SP+ desc for conf in by_conf: by_conf[conf].sort(key=lambda x: x["sp_overall"] or 0, reverse=True) return { "season": season, "total_teams": len(fbs_teams), "conferences": by_conf, } # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # TEAM DETAIL ENDPOINT # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/teams/{team_name}") def team_detail(team_name: str, season: int = 2026): """ Returns full team profile: schedule, ratings history, season stats. """ from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() fbs_teams = get_fbs_teams(db, season) conference = fbs_teams.get(team_name) # Schedule for requested season schedule_rows = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select( "id, season, week, season_type, start_date, neutral_site, " "conference_game, home_team, home_conference, away_team, " "away_conference, venue, home_points, away_points" ) .eq("season", season) .or_(f"home_team.eq.{team_name},away_team.eq.{team_name}") .order("week") ) schedule = [] wins = losses = 0 for g in schedule_rows: is_home = g["home_team"] == team_name opponent = g["away_team"] if is_home else g["home_team"] opp_conf = g["away_conference"] if is_home else g["home_conference"] has_score = g.get("home_points") is not None result = None team_pts = opp_pts = None if has_score: if is_home: team_pts = g["home_points"]; opp_pts = g["away_points"] else: team_pts = g["away_points"]; opp_pts = g["home_points"] if team_pts > opp_pts: result = "W"; wins += 1 elif team_pts < opp_pts: result = "L"; losses += 1 else: result = "T" raw_date = g.get("start_date", "") try: from datetime import datetime as _dt dt = _dt.fromisoformat(raw_date.replace("Z", "+00:00")) formatted_date = dt.strftime("%b %d").replace(" 0", " ") except: formatted_date = raw_date[:10] if raw_date else "TBD" schedule.append({ "game_id": str(g["id"]), "week": g.get("week"), "date": formatted_date, "opponent": opponent, "opp_conference": opp_conf, "is_home": is_home, "neutral_site": g.get("neutral_site", False), "conference_game": g.get("conference_game", False), "venue": g.get("venue"), "result": result, "team_points": team_pts, "opp_points": opp_pts, }) # Season stats — use current season if data exists, else fall back to prior season # This handles the 2026 preseason case automatically stat_cols = ("games_played,time_of_possession,top_pct,plays_per_game,seconds_per_play," "points_per_game,yards_per_game,yards_per_play,pass_yards_per_game," "rush_yards_per_game,first_downs_per_game,third_down_pct,red_zone_pct," "turnovers_per_game,points_allowed_per_game,yards_allowed_per_game," "yards_allowed_per_play,pass_yards_allowed_per_game,rush_yards_allowed_per_game," "opp_third_down_pct,opp_red_zone_pct,takeaways_per_game,opp_plays_per_game," "def_td_per_game,st_points_per_game,penalties_per_game,penalty_yards_per_game,team,season,week") # Try current season first stat_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_stats") .select(stat_cols) .eq("team", team_name) .eq("season", season) .order("week", desc=True) .limit(1) ) stat_season = season if not stat_rows: # Fall back to prior season (preseason scenario) stat_season = season - 1 stat_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_stats") .select(stat_cols) .eq("team", team_name) .eq("season", stat_season) .order("week", desc=True) .limit(1) ) stats = stat_rows[0] if stat_rows else {} # If points_allowed_per_game is null in the DB (common — the import doesn't # populate it from opponent box data), compute it on the fly from the # schedule's actual opponent-points data. if stats and (stats.get("points_allowed_per_game") is None): completed = [s for s in schedule if s.get("opp_points") is not None and (s.get("result") in ("W", "L", "T"))] if completed: total_opp_pts = sum(s["opp_points"] for s in completed) stats["points_allowed_per_game"] = round(total_opp_pts / len(completed), 2) # Pull ALL FBS team stats for same season/week for percentile rankings if stats: stat_week = stats.get("week") all_team_stats_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_stats") .select(stat_cols) .eq("season", stat_season) .eq("week", stat_week) ) # Filter to FBS teams only all_team_stats = [r for r in all_team_stats_rows if r.get("team") in fbs_teams] # Compute points_allowed_per_game on the fly for ANY team missing it # (the import inconsistently populates this — some teams have it, # most don't). Always pull season games and patch in missing values. teams_needing_compute = [t for t in all_team_stats if t.get("points_allowed_per_game") is None] if teams_needing_compute: season_games = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("home_team, away_team, home_points, away_points, season_type") .eq("season", stat_season) .not_.is_("home_points", "null") ) opp_pts_by_team = {} # {team: [opp_pts, ...]} for g in season_games: ht, at = g.get("home_team"), g.get("away_team") hp, ap = g.get("home_points"), g.get("away_points") if ht and ap is not None: opp_pts_by_team.setdefault(ht, []).append(ap) if at and hp is not None: opp_pts_by_team.setdefault(at, []).append(hp) for t in all_team_stats: if t.get("points_allowed_per_game") is None: name = t.get("team") if name in opp_pts_by_team and opp_pts_by_team[name]: pts_list = opp_pts_by_team[name] t["points_allowed_per_game"] = round(sum(pts_list) / len(pts_list), 2) else: all_team_stats = [] # ── Compute defensive stats from game_team_stats ── # Get all game IDs for this team in stat_season # ── Pull advanced stats for defensive metrics ── # game_team_stats has null team names, so we use advanced_stats instead. # FALLBACK: if no advanced_stats exist for the stat_season, walk back # one year at a time until we find data. This handles preseason scenarios # where 2026 has no advanced stats but 2025 does. adv_stat_season = stat_season adv_team_row = [] for try_season in [stat_season, stat_season - 1, stat_season - 2]: adv_team_row = fetch_all( db.table("advanced_stats") .select("off_success_rate,off_explosiveness,off_power_success,off_stuff_rate," "off_line_yards,def_success_rate,def_explosiveness,def_power_success," "def_stuff_rate,def_line_yards,def_havoc_total,def_havoc_front_seven,def_havoc_db") .eq("team", team_name) .eq("season", try_season) .limit(1) ) if adv_team_row: adv_stat_season = try_season break adv_team = adv_team_row[0] if adv_team_row else {} # Inject advanced defensive metrics into stats dict if adv_team: stats["def_success_rate"] = adv_team.get("def_success_rate") stats["def_explosiveness"] = adv_team.get("def_explosiveness") stats["def_havoc_total"] = adv_team.get("def_havoc_total") stats["def_stuff_rate"] = adv_team.get("def_stuff_rate") stats["off_success_rate"] = adv_team.get("off_success_rate") stats["off_explosiveness"] = adv_team.get("off_explosiveness") # Pull all FBS teams advanced stats for percentile ranking — use # whatever season worked above all_adv_rows = fetch_all( db.table("advanced_stats") .select("team,off_success_rate,off_explosiveness,off_power_success,off_stuff_rate," "off_line_yards,def_success_rate,def_explosiveness,def_power_success," "def_stuff_rate,def_line_yards,def_havoc_total,def_havoc_front_seven,def_havoc_db") .eq("season", adv_stat_season) ) # Inject into all_team_stats for percentile ranking adv_lookup = {r["team"]: r for r in all_adv_rows if r.get("team") in fbs_teams} for ts in all_team_stats: t = ts.get("team") if t in adv_lookup: a = adv_lookup[t] ts["def_success_rate"] = a.get("def_success_rate") ts["def_explosiveness"] = a.get("def_explosiveness") ts["def_havoc_total"] = a.get("def_havoc_total") ts["def_stuff_rate"] = a.get("def_stuff_rate") ts["off_success_rate"] = a.get("off_success_rate") ts["off_explosiveness"] = a.get("off_explosiveness") # Get opponent rows for those games (the other team's stats = our defense faced) # Compute percentile ranks for each stat # higher_better: True means higher value = better rank stat_meta = { "points_per_game": {"label": "Points / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "points_allowed_per_game": {"label": "Points Allowed / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "yards_per_game": {"label": "Yards / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "yards_per_play": {"label": "Yards / Play", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "pass_yards_per_game": {"label": "Pass Yards / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "rush_yards_per_game": {"label": "Rush Yards / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "yards_allowed_per_game": {"label": "Yards Allowed / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "yards_allowed_per_play": {"label": "Yards Allowed / Play", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "pass_yards_allowed_per_game": {"label": "Pass Yards Allowed", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "rush_yards_allowed_per_game": {"label": "Rush Yards Allowed", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "first_downs_per_game": {"label": "First Downs / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "third_down_pct": {"label": "3rd Down Conv %", "higher_better": True, "unit": "%"}, "opp_third_down_pct": {"label": "Opp 3rd Down Conv %", "higher_better": False, "unit": "%"}, "red_zone_pct": {"label": "Red Zone Score %", "higher_better": True, "unit": "%"}, "opp_red_zone_pct": {"label": "Opp Red Zone Score %", "higher_better": False, "unit": "%"}, "top_pct": {"label": "Time of Possession %", "higher_better": True, "unit": "%"}, "plays_per_game": {"label": "Plays / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "opp_plays_per_game": {"label": "Opp Plays / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "turnovers_per_game": {"label": "Turnovers / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "takeaways_per_game": {"label": "Takeaways / Game", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "penalties_per_game": {"label": "Penalties / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "penalty_yards_per_game": {"label": "Penalty Yards / Game", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "st_points_per_game": {"label": "Special Teams Pts / Game","higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "seconds_per_play": {"label": "Seconds / Play (Pace)", "higher_better": False, "unit": "s"}, # Advanced defensive metrics "def_success_rate": {"label": "Def Success Rate", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "def_explosiveness": {"label": "Def Explosiveness", "higher_better": False, "unit": ""}, "def_havoc_total": {"label": "Def Havoc Rate", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "def_stuff_rate": {"label": "Def Stuff Rate", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, # Advanced offensive metrics "off_success_rate": {"label": "Off Success Rate", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, "off_explosiveness": {"label": "Off Explosiveness", "higher_better": True, "unit": ""}, } stat_ranks = {} n = len(all_team_stats) for col, meta in stat_meta.items(): vals = [(r.get("team"), r.get(col)) for r in all_team_stats if r.get(col) is not None] if not vals: continue vals.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=meta["higher_better"]) team_rank = next((i+1 for i, (t, _) in enumerate(vals) if t == team_name), None) if team_rank is not None: pct = round((1 - (team_rank - 1) / max(len(vals) - 1, 1)) * 100) stat_ranks[col] = { "rank": team_rank, "of": len(vals), "percentile": pct, "value": stats.get(col), "label": meta["label"], "unit": meta["unit"], "higher_better": meta["higher_better"], } # Power ratings history (last 3 seasons) rating_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_ratings") .select("season, sp_overall, sp_offense, sp_defense, elo") .eq("team", team_name) .in_("season", [season-1, season-2, season-3]) ) ratings_by_season = {} for r in rating_rows: s = r.get("season") if s not in ratings_by_season: ratings_by_season[s] = {"sp_overall": None, "sp_offense": None, "sp_defense": None, "elo": None} if r.get("sp_overall") is not None: ratings_by_season[s].update({ "sp_overall": r["sp_overall"], "sp_offense": r.get("sp_offense"), "sp_defense": r.get("sp_defense"), }) if r.get("elo") is not None: ratings_by_season[s]["elo"] = r["elo"] return { "team": team_name, "conference": conference, "season": season, "stat_season": stat_season, "record": {"wins": wins, "losses": losses}, "schedule": schedule, "stats": stats, "stat_ranks": stat_ranks, "ratings": ratings_by_season, } # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # PLAYER DATA — PIPELINE + RANKINGS # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.post("/admin/load-player-stats") def load_player_stats(season: int = 2025): """ Pull player stats + returning production from CFBD and store in Supabase. Creates/upserts player_stats and player_info tables. Run once for historical, then weekly during season. """ import os, requests, time try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() CFBD_KEY = os.environ.get("CFBD_API_KEY", "") if not CFBD_KEY: return {"error": "CFBD_API_KEY not set"} HEADERS = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {CFBD_KEY}"} BASE = "https://api.collegefootballdata.com" def cfbd_get(path, params=None): try: r = requests.get(f"{BASE}{path}", headers=HEADERS, params=params or {}, timeout=30) return r.json() if r.status_code == 200 else [] except Exception: return [] # FBS conferences filter FBS_CONFS = [ "ACC", "Big 12", "Big Ten", "SEC", "American Athletic", "Mountain West", "Sun Belt", "Conference USA", "Mid-American", "Pac-12", "FBS Independents" ] # ── Pull passing stats ── passing = cfbd_get("/stats/player/season", { "year": season, "category": "passing", "seasonType": "regular" }) # ── Pull rushing stats ── rushing = cfbd_get("/stats/player/season", { "year": season, "category": "rushing", "seasonType": "regular" }) # ── Pull receiving stats ── receiving = cfbd_get("/stats/player/season", { "year": season, "category": "receiving", "seasonType": "regular" }) # ── Pull defensive stats ── defense = cfbd_get("/stats/player/season", { "year": season, "category": "defensive", "seasonType": "regular" }) # ── Pull returning production ── returning_data = cfbd_get("/player/returning", {"year": season + 1}) # ── Build player_id -> info lookup from returning data ── returning_lookup = {} for r in (returning_data or []): pid = str(r.get("playerId", "")) if pid: returning_lookup[pid] = { "returning": True, "eligibility": r.get("eligibility"), } # ── Aggregate all stats by player ── players = {} # player_id -> merged stats def merge_stat(rows, stat_map): for row in (rows or []): pid = str(row.get("playerId", "")) if not pid: continue conf = row.get("conference", "") if conf not in FBS_CONFS: continue if pid not in players: players[pid] = { "player_id": pid, "name": row.get("player", ""), "team": row.get("team", ""), "conference": conf, "position": row.get("position", ""), "season": season, } val = row.get("stat") try: val = float(val) if val is not None else None except: val = None col = stat_map.get(row.get("statType", "")) if col and val is not None: players[pid][col] = val # Passing stat types passing_map = { "YDS": "passing_yards", "TD": "passing_tds", "INT": "interceptions", "COMPLETIONS": "completions", "ATT": "passing_att", "PCT": "completion_pct", "YPA": "yards_per_attempt", "RATING": "passer_rating", } # Rushing rushing_map = { "YDS": "rushing_yards", "TD": "rushing_tds", "CAR": "rushing_att", "AVG": "yards_per_carry", "LONG": "rushing_long", } # Receiving receiving_map = { "YDS": "receiving_yards", "TD": "receiving_tds", "REC": "receptions", "AVG": "yards_per_reception", "LONG": "receiving_long", } # Defensive defense_map = { "TOT": "tackles", "SOLO": "solo_tackles", "SACKS": "sacks", "TFL": "tackles_for_loss", "INT": "def_interceptions", "PD": "passes_broken_up", "QB HUR": "qb_hurries", "TD": "def_tds", } merge_stat(passing, passing_map) merge_stat(rushing, rushing_map) merge_stat(receiving, receiving_map) merge_stat(defense, defense_map) # ── Add returning status ── for pid, p in players.items(): ret = returning_lookup.get(pid, {}) p["returning_2026"] = ret.get("returning", False) p["eligibility"] = ret.get("eligibility") # ── Upsert to Supabase ── rows = list(players.values()) upserted = 0 batch_size = 100 for i in range(0, len(rows), batch_size): batch = rows[i:i+batch_size] try: db.table("player_stats").upsert( batch, on_conflict="player_id,season" ).execute() upserted += len(batch) except Exception as e: # Table may not exist yet — return schema for manual creation return { "error": f"Upsert failed: {str(e)}", "hint": "Run the SQL migration first to create player_stats table", "sql": """ CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS player_stats ( id BIGSERIAL PRIMARY KEY, player_id TEXT NOT NULL, name TEXT, team TEXT, conference TEXT, position TEXT, season INT, passing_yards FLOAT, passing_tds FLOAT, interceptions FLOAT, completions FLOAT, passing_att FLOAT, completion_pct FLOAT, yards_per_attempt FLOAT, passer_rating FLOAT, rushing_yards FLOAT, rushing_tds FLOAT, rushing_att FLOAT, yards_per_carry FLOAT, rushing_long FLOAT, receiving_yards FLOAT, receiving_tds FLOAT, receptions FLOAT, yards_per_reception FLOAT, receiving_long FLOAT, tackles FLOAT, solo_tackles FLOAT, sacks FLOAT, tackles_for_loss FLOAT, def_interceptions FLOAT, passes_broken_up FLOAT, qb_hurries FLOAT, def_tds FLOAT, returning_2026 BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE, eligibility TEXT, created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(), updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(), UNIQUE(player_id, season) ); CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_player_stats_season ON player_stats(season); CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_player_stats_team ON player_stats(team); CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_player_stats_position ON player_stats(position); """ } time.sleep(0.1) return { "season": season, "players_loaded": upserted, "total_players": len(rows), "returning_matched": sum(1 for p in rows if p.get("returning_2026")), } except Exception as e: import traceback return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/players/rankings") def player_rankings( season: int = 2025, position: str = None, team: str = None, conference: str = None, returning_only: bool = False, limit: int = 200, ): """ Hybrid player rankings: - Skill positions (QB/RB/WR/TE): ranked by player_value, driven by prior-season PPA totals from player_seasons table. - Non-skill positions (DL/EDGE/LB/DB): ranked by percentile composite of actual production counting stats from player_stats table (sacks, TFLs, tackles, INTs, PBUs, etc.). This gives us real production rankings everywhere, not recruiting proxies. """ from pipeline.db import get_db from bisect import bisect_right db = get_db() # Position group resolution SKILL_POS_GROUPS = { "QB": ["QB", "Quarterback"], "RB": ["RB", "HB", "FB", "TB", "Running Back", "Fullback"], "WR": ["WR", "Wide Receiver"], "TE": ["TE", "Tight End"], } NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS = { "DL": ["DL", "DT", "NT", "DE"], "EDGE": ["EDGE", "OLB"], # EDGE players often live under OLB in old data "LB": ["LB", "ILB", "MLB"], "DB": ["DB", "CB", "S", "SS", "FS", "NB"], } ALL_GROUPS = {**SKILL_POS_GROUPS, **NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS} pos_group = position.upper() if position else None if pos_group == "SKILL": skill_positions = (SKILL_POS_GROUPS["QB"] + SKILL_POS_GROUPS["RB"] + SKILL_POS_GROUPS["WR"] + SKILL_POS_GROUPS["TE"]) nonskill_positions = [] elif pos_group in SKILL_POS_GROUPS: skill_positions = SKILL_POS_GROUPS[pos_group] nonskill_positions = [] elif pos_group in NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS: skill_positions = [] nonskill_positions = NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS[pos_group] else: # No filter: pull all groups skill_positions = sum(SKILL_POS_GROUPS.values(), []) nonskill_positions = sum(NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS.values(), []) # ─── SKILL POSITION RANKINGS (PPA-based) ──────────────────── # IMPORTANT: a player's PPA score comes from their PRIOR season, # but we want to show them on their CURRENT team. Build a current-team # lookup that uses the most-recent player_seasons row for each player. current_team_lookup = {} # {player_id: (current_team, current_conference, current_pos)} try: # Pull all 2026 player_seasons rows; these reflect new rosters after transfer portal current_rows = fetch_all( db.table("player_seasons") .select("player_id, team, conference, position") .eq("season", season + 1) ) for r in current_rows: pid = r.get("player_id") if pid: current_team_lookup[pid] = (r.get("team"), r.get("conference"), r.get("position")) except Exception: pass skill_scored = [] if skill_positions: q = (db.table("player_seasons") .select("player_id, season, team, conference, position, jersey, " "usage_overall, ppa_total_all, ppa_avg_all, " "ppa_total_pass, ppa_total_rush, player_value") .eq("season", season) .not_.is_("player_value", "null") .in_("position", skill_positions)) # NOTE: team/conference filters applied in Python AFTER mapping # players to their current team, since a transferred player may match # the requested team only by their CURRENT (next-season) roster. skill_rows = fetch_all(q) # Get names skill_pids = list({r["player_id"] for r in skill_rows if r.get("player_id")}) names_by_pid = {} BATCH = 500 for i in range(0, len(skill_pids), BATCH): chunk = skill_pids[i:i+BATCH] name_rows = (db.table("players") .select("player_id, first_name, last_name") .in_("player_id", chunk).execute().data) or [] for nr in name_rows: names_by_pid[nr["player_id"]] = ( f"{(nr.get('first_name') or '').strip()} " f"{(nr.get('last_name') or '').strip()}" ).strip() # Pos group resolver def get_skill_group(pos): if not pos: return "OTHER" for g, positions in SKILL_POS_GROUPS.items(): if pos in positions: return g return "OTHER" # Normalize player_value (range ±7) to 0-100 score for UI def norm_pv(pv): if pv is None: return 0 return max(0, min(100, round((pv + 7) / 14 * 100, 1))) for row in skill_rows: pid = row.get("player_id") pv = row.get("player_value") if pv is None: continue # Use CURRENT team/conference/position if the player is still active. # If no current-season entry, fall back to prior team (player likely # exhausted eligibility or is unsigned — show prior team). cur = current_team_lookup.get(pid) if cur and cur[0]: current_team = cur[0] current_conference = cur[1] or row.get("conference") current_position = cur[2] or row.get("position") still_active = True else: current_team = row.get("team") current_conference = row.get("conference") current_position = row.get("position") still_active = False # If user filtered by team, only include players whose CURRENT team matches if team and current_team != team: continue if conference and current_conference != conference: continue skill_scored.append({ "player_id": pid, "name": names_by_pid.get(pid, "?"), "team": current_team, "conference": current_conference, "position": current_position, "position_group": get_skill_group(current_position), "season": season, "score": norm_pv(pv), "player_value": round(float(pv), 2), "ppa_total": row.get("ppa_total_all"), "ppa_avg": row.get("ppa_avg_all"), "ppa_total_pass": row.get("ppa_total_pass"), "ppa_total_rush": row.get("ppa_total_rush"), "usage_overall": row.get("usage_overall"), "jersey": row.get("jersey"), "prior_team": row.get("team") if row.get("team") != current_team else None, "transferred": row.get("team") != current_team and still_active, "still_active": still_active, }) # ─── NON-SKILL POSITION RANKINGS (counting stats) ─────────── nonskill_scored = [] if nonskill_positions: # Weights per group (same as the original endpoint) WEIGHTS = { "DL": {"sacks": 0.35, "tackles_for_loss": 0.30, "tackles": 0.20, "qb_hurries": 0.15}, "EDGE": {"sacks": 0.35, "tackles_for_loss": 0.30, "tackles": 0.20, "qb_hurries": 0.15}, "LB": {"tackles": 0.40, "tackles_for_loss": 0.25, "sacks": 0.15, "def_interceptions": 0.10, "passes_broken_up": 0.10}, "DB": {"def_interceptions": 0.35, "passes_broken_up": 0.30, "tackles": 0.25, "def_tds": 0.10}, } q = db.table("player_stats").select("*").eq("season", season) q = q.in_("position", nonskill_positions) # NOTE: team/conference filters applied in Python AFTER mapping to current team ns_rows = fetch_all(q) def get_ns_group(pos): if not pos: return "OTHER" for g, positions in NONSKILL_POS_GROUPS.items(): if pos in positions: return g return "OTHER" # Collect stat distributions per group group_stats = {} for row in ns_rows: g = get_ns_group(row.get("position", "")) if g not in group_stats: group_stats[g] = {} weights = WEIGHTS.get(g, {}) for stat in weights: val = row.get(stat) if val is not None: group_stats[g].setdefault(stat, []).append(float(val)) for g in group_stats: for k in group_stats[g]: group_stats[g][k].sort() def percentile_score(val, sorted_vals): if val is None or not sorted_vals: return 0 rank = bisect_right(sorted_vals, val) return rank / len(sorted_vals) for row in ns_rows: g = get_ns_group(row.get("position", "")) weights = WEIGHTS.get(g, {}) if not weights: continue total_score = 0.0; total_weight = 0.0 for stat, w in weights.items(): val = row.get(stat) if val is None: continue all_vals = group_stats.get(g, {}).get(stat, []) total_score += percentile_score(float(val), all_vals) * w total_weight += w if total_weight == 0: continue composite = round((total_score / total_weight) * 100, 1) # Apply current-team mapping (handles transfers) pid = row.get("player_id") cur = current_team_lookup.get(pid) if cur and cur[0]: current_team = cur[0] current_conference = cur[1] or row.get("conference") current_position = cur[2] or row.get("position") still_active = True else: current_team = row.get("team") current_conference = row.get("conference") current_position = row.get("position") still_active = False # Apply team/conference filters in Python if team and current_team != team: continue if conference and current_conference != conference: continue nonskill_scored.append({ "player_id": pid, "name": row.get("name"), "team": current_team, "conference": current_conference, "position": current_position, "position_group": g, "season": season, "score": composite, "tackles": row.get("tackles"), "sacks": row.get("sacks"), "tackles_for_loss": row.get("tackles_for_loss"), "def_interceptions": row.get("def_interceptions"), "passes_broken_up": row.get("passes_broken_up"), "qb_hurries": row.get("qb_hurries"), "def_tds": row.get("def_tds"), "returning_2026": row.get("returning_2026", False), "prior_team": row.get("team") if row.get("team") != current_team else None, "transferred": row.get("team") != current_team and still_active, "still_active": still_active, }) # Merge and sort scored = skill_scored + nonskill_scored scored.sort(key=lambda x: -x["score"]) # returning_2026: a player is "returning" if they appear on a 2026 roster. # The skill players already have `still_active` set above (via the # current_team_lookup). For non-skill players we trust the load-time flag. # FALLBACK: if no 2026 roster data exists at all, treat everyone as # potentially returning — don't drop them all from the page. has_any_2026_roster_data = bool(current_team_lookup) # set earlier for p in skill_scored: if "still_active" in p: p["returning_2026"] = p["still_active"] if has_any_2026_roster_data else True elif "returning_2026" not in p: p["returning_2026"] = True if not has_any_2026_roster_data else False # For non-skill, the returning_2026 flag was loaded with the player_stats # rows. But if we have no 2026 data at all, override to true so the page # isn't empty. if not has_any_2026_roster_data: for p in nonskill_scored: p["returning_2026"] = True if returning_only: scored = [p for p in scored if p.get("returning_2026")] # Final rank for i, p in enumerate(scored): p["rank"] = i + 1 if not scored: return { "season": season, "position": position, "total": 0, "players": [], "full": [], "hint": "No players found. For skill positions ensure /admin/compute-player-values has run. For non-skill ensure /admin/load-player-stats has run.", } return { "season": season, "position": position or "ALL", "returning_only": returning_only, "total": len(scored), "players": scored[:limit], "full": scored, } # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # RETURNING PLAYERS BACKFILL # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # Players who declared for the 2026 NFL Draft and will NOT be returning to # college football in 2026, even if they have remaining eligibility. Source: # ESPN's official list of 63 underclassmen who declared by the Jan 14 deadline. # https://www.espn.com/nfl/draft2026/story/_/id/47600173/ # # Player IDs match CFBD's player_id format (ESPN and CFBD use the same IDs). NFL_DECLARED_2026_IDS = { "4685479", "4685502", "4685512", "4685518", "4685522", "4685549", "4685564", "4689117", "4691138", "4695705", "4816090", "4832793", "4832800", "4832922", "4832955", "4833029", "4833376", "4838270", "4868598", "4869533", "4870596", "4870598", "4870612", "4870653", "4870694", "4870706", "4870707", "4870723", "4870795", "4870805", "4870808", "4870847", "4870866", "4870886", "4870893", "4870953", "4870976", "4870988", "4870998", "4871023", "4871063", "4880273", "4880281", "4896353", "4917859", "4921249", "4921438", "4950400", "4950551", "4954445", "5076652", "5076951", "5080699", "5081432", "5081886", "5083315", "5084956", "5085189", "5091739", "5093004", "5150419", "5157289", "5218510", } # Late declarers from Indiana/Miami (CFP teams had until Jan 23 to declare, # so they're not in the ESPN list which was published Jan 15) and other # players drafted in 2026 who were underclassmen. Looked up by name+team # from player_stats at runtime since their CFBD IDs aren't documented. NFL_DECLARED_2026_LATE = [ # Indiana (national championship participant) ("Fernando Mendoza", "Indiana"), # #1 overall - Raiders ("Omar Cooper Jr.", "Indiana"), # Round 1 - Jets ("Elijah Sarratt", "Indiana"), # Round 4 - Ravens ("Aiden Fisher", "Indiana"), # Round 7 - Texans # Miami (national championship participant) ("Rueben Bain Jr.", "Miami"), # Round 1 - Buccaneers ("Akeem Mesidor", "Miami"), # Round 1 - Chargers # Other 2026 underclassmen draftees not in the ESPN 63 ("Max Iheanachor", "Arizona State"), ("Malachi Lawrence", "UCF"), ("Chris Johnson", "San Diego State"), ("Keylan Rutledge", "Georgia Tech"), ("Treydan Stukes", "Arizona"), ("Keyron Crawford", "Auburn"), ("Trey Zuhn III", "Texas A&M"), ("Mike Washington Jr.","Arkansas"), ("Dalton Johnson", "Arizona"), ("Hezekiah Masses", "California"), # CFBD uses "California" not "Cal" ("Malik Benson", "Oregon"), ("Brandon Cleveland", "NC State"), ("Matthew Hibner", "SMU"), ("Chandler Rivers", "Duke"), ("Josh Cuevas", "Alabama"), ("Adam Randall", "Clemson"), ("Rayshaun Benny", "Michigan"), ("Evan Beerntsen", "Northwestern"), ] @app.get("/admin/backfill-returning-production") def backfill_returning_production(season: int = 2025): """ Backfills the returning_2026 flag in player_stats. Approach: 2026 rosters do not exist in CFBD until ~July of the new year. Instead we use the 2025 roster's `year` field (academic year: 1=Freshman, 2=Sophomore, 3=Junior, 4=Senior, 5+=fifth-year/grad). Anyone with year < 4 is treated as returning. Seniors (year >= 4) are treated as departing. This is an approximation — it can't account for the transfer portal or early NFL departures — but it's the best signal available before the next-season roster is published. Re-run after CFBD publishes the 2026 roster for an exact answer. Run anytime after loading player_stats. Safe to re-run. Usage: GET /admin/backfill-returning-production?season=2025 """ import os, requests, traceback try: from pipeline.db import get_db db = get_db() CFBD_KEY = os.environ.get("CFBD_API_KEY", "") if not CFBD_KEY: return {"error": "CFBD_API_KEY not set"} HEADERS = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {CFBD_KEY}"} BASE = "https://api.collegefootballdata.com" # Try the next-season roster first — if CFBD has it, that's the truth. next_season = season + 1 try: r = requests.get(f"{BASE}/roster", headers=HEADERS, params={"year": next_season}, timeout=60) next_roster = r.json() if r.status_code == 200 else [] except Exception: next_roster = [] used_next_roster = bool(next_roster) returning_ids = set() if used_next_roster: # Best case: real next-season roster exists for player in next_roster: pid = player.get("id") if pid is not None: returning_ids.add(str(pid)) else: # Fall back: pull current-season roster and use the `year` field try: r = requests.get(f"{BASE}/roster", headers=HEADERS, params={"year": season}, timeout=60) if r.status_code != 200: return { "error": f"CFBD /roster?year={season} returned status {r.status_code}", "response_preview": r.text[:300], } current_roster = r.json() or [] except Exception as e: return {"error": f"CFBD request failed: {str(e)}"} if not current_roster: return { "error": f"CFBD returned no roster data for year {season} or {next_season}", } # Year field: 1=FR, 2=SO, 3=JR, 4=SR, 5+=fifth-year/grad # Treat year < 4 as returning. Seniors (4) and beyond do not return # by default; some 5th-year guys come back, but we cannot tell from # this data alone. Conservative: assume year >= 4 means departing. for player in current_roster: pid = player.get("id") yr = player.get("year") if pid is None or yr is None: continue try: yr_int = int(yr) except (TypeError, ValueError): continue if yr_int < 4: returning_ids.add(str(pid)) if not returning_ids: return { "error": "Could not derive any returning player IDs", "used_next_roster": used_next_roster, } # ── NFL EXCLUSIONS ─────────────────────────────────────────────── # Remove underclassmen who declared for the 2026 NFL Draft. Two # sources: the ESPN-published list of 63 IDs (Jan 14 deadline) and # the late Indiana/Miami CFP declarers we look up by name+team. nfl_excluded_ids = set(NFL_DECLARED_2026_IDS) late_lookup_resolved = 0 late_lookup_missed = [] # Resolve late declarers by name + team via the current roster # we already loaded (or pull it fresh if we used next_season_roster) try: if used_next_roster: # We didn't load current_roster above — pull it now for name lookup r = requests.get(f"{BASE}/roster", headers=HEADERS, params={"year": season}, timeout=60) lookup_roster = r.json() if r.status_code == 200 else [] else: lookup_roster = current_roster except Exception: lookup_roster = [] if lookup_roster: # Build name+team -> id index (lowercased, stripped) name_index = {} for p in lookup_roster: pid = p.get("id") first = (p.get("firstName") or "").strip() last = (p.get("lastName") or "").strip() team = (p.get("team") or "").strip() if pid and first and last and team: full = f"{first} {last}".lower().strip() key = (full, team.lower()) name_index[key] = str(pid) for full_name, team_name in NFL_DECLARED_2026_LATE: key = (full_name.lower().strip(), team_name.lower().strip()) pid = name_index.get(key) if pid: nfl_excluded_ids.add(pid) late_lookup_resolved += 1 else: late_lookup_missed.append(f"{full_name} ({team_name})") # Subtract NFL declarees from the returning set nfl_excluded_from_returning = returning_ids & nfl_excluded_ids returning_ids = returning_ids - nfl_excluded_ids # Pull all current player_stats rows for the given season all_stats = fetch_all( db.table("player_stats") .select("player_id") .eq("season", season) ) existing_ids = {r["player_id"] for r in all_stats if r.get("player_id")} # Intersection: in our DB AND flagged as returning ids_to_mark = list(existing_ids & returning_ids) ids_not_returning = list(existing_ids - returning_ids) # Step 1: reset everyone in the season to False try: db.table("player_stats") \ .update({"returning_2026": False}) \ .eq("season", season) \ .execute() except Exception as e: return {"error": f"Reset step failed: {str(e)}"} # Step 2: mark returning players as True, in batches marked = 0 BATCH = 100 for i in range(0, len(ids_to_mark), BATCH): batch = ids_to_mark[i:i+BATCH] try: db.table("player_stats") \ .update({"returning_2026": True}) \ .eq("season", season) \ .in_("player_id", batch) \ .execute() marked += len(batch) except Exception as e: return { "error": f"Update step failed at batch {i}: {str(e)}", "marked_so_far": marked, } return { "season": season, "method": "next_season_roster" if used_next_roster else "current_year_field", "note": None if used_next_roster else "2026 roster not yet published; using year<4 from 2025 roster as proxy", "returning_ids_total": len(returning_ids), "players_in_db": len(existing_ids), "marked_returning": marked, "marked_not_returning": len(ids_not_returning), "nfl_exclusions": { "espn_list_size": len(NFL_DECLARED_2026_IDS), "late_declarers_total": len(NFL_DECLARED_2026_LATE), "late_declarers_resolved": late_lookup_resolved, "late_declarers_missed": late_lookup_missed, "removed_from_returning": len(nfl_excluded_from_returning), }, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} @app.get("/admin/debug-cfbd-roster") def debug_cfbd_roster(year: int = 2026, team: str = "Indiana"): """ Diagnostic — probes the CFBD /roster endpoint several ways so we can see what data is actually available right now. Returns response status, count, and a sample row for each variation. """ import os, requests, traceback try: CFBD_KEY = os.environ.get("CFBD_API_KEY", "") if not CFBD_KEY: return {"error": "CFBD_API_KEY not set"} HEADERS = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {CFBD_KEY}"} BASE = "https://api.collegefootballdata.com" def probe(label, params): try: r = requests.get(f"{BASE}/roster", headers=HEADERS, params=params, timeout=30) if r.status_code != 200: return { "label": label, "params": params, "status": r.status_code, "preview": r.text[:200], } data = r.json() or [] return { "label": label, "params": params, "status": 200, "count": len(data), "sample": data[0] if data else None, } except Exception as e: return {"label": label, "params": params, "error": str(e)} results = [] # Try the year we asked about (default 2026) results.append(probe(f"year={year} only", {"year": year})) # Try the prior year results.append(probe(f"year={year - 1} only", {"year": year - 1})) # Try the year + a specific team results.append(probe(f"year={year} + team={team}", {"year": year, "team": team})) # Try the prior year + team results.append(probe(f"year={year - 1} + team={team}", {"year": year - 1, "team": team})) # Try team only results.append(probe(f"team={team} only", {"team": team})) return { "cfbd_key_present": bool(CFBD_KEY), "results": results, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # GAME DETAIL PAGE (single game, all the data) # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/game/{game_id}") def game_detail(game_id: int): """ Returns everything needed to render a single game page: - matchup (teams, date, venue, conferences) - final score (if played) - market line (spread, total, moneylines) - ensemble prediction (4 component models + weighted ensemble) - our picks (spread, total, moneyline) with tiers - pick grading (won/lost/push) if game is played - team-stat comparison for data bars (using the most recent season we have stats for: 2025 if 2026 games aren't yet played) Public endpoint. Frontend handles auth-gating for unplayed games. """ import traceback try: from pipeline.db import get_db from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats from models.adjustments import compute_adjustments, build_games_index from models.ensemble_model import _combine db = get_db() # 1. Fetch the game itself game_rows = fetch_all( db.table("games").select("*").eq("id", game_id).limit(1) ) if not game_rows: return {"error": f"Game {game_id} not found"} game = game_rows[0] ht = game["home_team"] at = game["away_team"] season = game["season"] week = game["week"] ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) is_played = game.get("home_points") is not None # 2. Load model data (uses current + prior season) all_s = [season, season - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, start_date, " "neutral_site, conference_game, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) games_idx = build_games_index(all_games_raw) # 3. Fetch market line for this matchup line_rows = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, over_under, " "opening_spread, opening_over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline") .eq("provider", "Bovada") .eq("season", season) .eq("week", week) .eq("home_team", ht) .eq("away_team", at) ) line = line_rows[0] if line_rows else None _ol = get_opening_line(line) if line else {} mkt_spread = _ol.get("spread") if line else None mkt_total = _ol.get("over_under") if line else None home_ml = _ol.get("home_moneyline") if line else None away_ml = _ol.get("away_moneyline") if line else None # 4. Run all 4 component models + ensemble sp_pred = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo_pred = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa_pred = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) advanced_pred = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats) home_adv = adv_stats.get((ht, season)) or adv_stats.get((ht, season - 1)) away_adv = adv_stats.get((at, season)) or adv_stats.get((at, season - 1)) adj = compute_adjustments(game, games_idx, home_adv, away_adv) pred = _combine(ht, at, season, week, ns, sp_pred, elo_pred, ppa_pred, advanced_pred, mkt_spread, mkt_total, home_ml, away_ml, adj=adj) # 5. Grade picks if game is played grading = None if is_played and pred: hp = game.get("home_points") or 0 ap = game.get("away_points") or 0 actual_margin = hp - ap # home perspective: positive = home won actual_total = hp + ap grading = { "home_points": hp, "away_points": ap, "actual_margin": actual_margin, "actual_total": actual_total, "winner": "home" if actual_margin > 0 else ("away" if actual_margin < 0 else "tie"), } # Grade spread pick if pred.get("spread_pick") and mkt_spread is not None: # spread_pick like "Iowa +2" or "Cincinnati -3" picked_home = (pred["spread_pick"].startswith(ht) or (ht.lower() in pred["spread_pick"].lower() and at.lower() not in pred["spread_pick"].lower())) if picked_home: cover = actual_margin > -mkt_spread push = actual_margin == -mkt_spread else: cover = actual_margin < -mkt_spread push = actual_margin == -mkt_spread grading["spread_result"] = "push" if push else ("won" if cover else "lost") # Grade total pick if pred.get("ou_pick") and mkt_total is not None: # ou_pick is "Over 55" or "Under 55" is_over = pred["ou_pick"].lower().startswith("over") if is_over: hit = actual_total > mkt_total else: hit = actual_total < mkt_total push = actual_total == mkt_total grading["ou_result"] = "push" if push else ("won" if hit else "lost") # Grade moneyline pick if pred.get("ml_pick"): picked_home_ml = pred["ml_pick"].startswith(ht) or (ht.lower() in pred["ml_pick"].lower() and at.lower() not in pred["ml_pick"].lower()) won_ml = (picked_home_ml and actual_margin > 0) or (not picked_home_ml and actual_margin < 0) grading["ml_result"] = "won" if won_ml else ("push" if actual_margin == 0 else "lost") # 6. Team stats for data bars - use most recent completed season stats_season = season if is_played else (season - 1) def team_stats(team): ratings_rows = fetch_all( db.table("team_ratings").select("*") .eq("team", team).eq("season", stats_season).limit(1) ) ppa_rows = fetch_all( db.table("ppa_season").select("*") .eq("team", team).eq("season", stats_season).limit(1) ) adv_rows = fetch_all( db.table("advanced_stats").select("*") .eq("team", team).eq("season", stats_season).limit(1) ) r = ratings_rows[0] if ratings_rows else {} p = ppa_rows[0] if ppa_rows else {} a = adv_rows[0] if adv_rows else {} return { "team": team, "sp_rating": r.get("sp_overall") or r.get("rating"), "ppa_offense": p.get("ppa_overall_offense"), "ppa_defense": p.get("ppa_overall_defense"), "explosiveness": a.get("explosiveness_offense") or a.get("explosiveness"), "havoc": a.get("havoc_defense_total") or a.get("havoc"), "success_rate": a.get("success_rate_offense") or a.get("success_rate"), "stuff_rate": a.get("stuff_rate_offense") or a.get("stuff_rate"), "ppa_pass": p.get("ppa_passing_offense"), "ppa_rush": p.get("ppa_rushing_offense"), } return { "game_id": game_id, "is_played": is_played, "matchup": { "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "home_conference": game.get("home_conference"), "away_conference": game.get("away_conference"), "season": season, "week": week, "start_date": game.get("start_date"), "venue": game.get("venue"), "neutral_site": ns, "season_type": game.get("season_type"), }, "market": { "spread": mkt_spread, "over_under": mkt_total, "home_moneyline": home_ml, "away_moneyline": away_ml, "has_line": line is not None, }, "models": { "sp": sp_pred, "elo": elo_pred, "ppa": ppa_pred, "advanced": advanced_pred, }, "ensemble": pred, "grading": grading, "team_stats": { "stats_season": stats_season, "home": team_stats(ht), "away": team_stats(at), }, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # CONFIGURABLE BACKTEST ENDPOINT — for tuning model + roster dials together # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/backtest-tune") def backtest_tune( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", # Roster dials roster_enabled: bool = True, roster_mult: float = 1.0, roster_total_mult: float = 1.0, roster_qb_only: bool = False, roster_skill_only: bool = False, roster_min_threshold: float = 0.0, roster_cap: float = 10.0, # Existing adjustment dials bye_mult: float = 1.0, total_adj_mult: float = 1.0, # Individual adjustment component dials (0 = off, 1 = default) bye_spread_mult: float = 1.0, bye_total_mult: float = 1.0, short_week_spread_mult: float = 1.0, short_week_total_mult: float = 1.0, non_conf_total_mult: float = 1.0, exp_havoc_mult: float = 1.0, early_week_conf_mult: float = 1.0, # Ensemble weight dials sp_weight_mult: float = 1.0, elo_weight_mult: float = 1.0, ppa_weight_mult: float = 1.0, advanced_weight_mult: float = 1.0, tempo_weight_mult: float = 1.0, # Spread tier thresholds spread_ap_min_edge: float = 2.0, spread_ap_max_edge: float = 6.0, spread_ap_min_agree: int = 2, spread_ap_max_agree: int = 3, spread_a_min_edge: float = 2.0, spread_a_min_agree: int = 2, spread_a_alt_edge: float = 3.0, spread_a_alt_agree: int = 4, spread_b_min_edge: float = 1.0, spread_b_min_agree: int = 2, spread_late_max_edge: float = 5.0, # Over/Under tier thresholds ou_ap_min_edge: float = 6.0, ou_a_min_edge: float = 3.0, ou_b_min_edge: float = 5.0, # Moneyline tier thresholds ml_ap_edge: float = 0.15, ml_ap_min_implied: float = 0.35, ml_ap_max_implied: float = 0.65, ml_ap_min_agree: int = 3, # Line choice — True = opening (what users bet against), False = closing use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Configurable ensemble backtest. Defaults reflect production behavior: opening line + all five models including tempo + all current tier thresholds. Examples: /admin/backtest-tune # production behavior /admin/backtest-tune?roster_enabled=false # baseline w/o roster /admin/backtest-tune?use_opening_line=false # closing line view /admin/backtest-tune?tempo_weight_mult=0 # disable tempo """ import traceback try: from models.ensemble_model import backtest_ensemble_tunable seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] cfg = { "roster_enabled": roster_enabled, "roster_mult": roster_mult, "roster_total_mult": roster_total_mult, "roster_qb_only": roster_qb_only, "roster_skill_only": roster_skill_only, "roster_min_threshold": roster_min_threshold, "roster_cap": roster_cap, "bye_mult": bye_mult, "total_adj_mult": total_adj_mult, "bye_spread_mult": bye_spread_mult, "bye_total_mult": bye_total_mult, "short_week_spread_mult": short_week_spread_mult, "short_week_total_mult": short_week_total_mult, "non_conf_total_mult": non_conf_total_mult, "exp_havoc_mult": exp_havoc_mult, "early_week_conf_mult": early_week_conf_mult, "sp_weight_mult": sp_weight_mult, "elo_weight_mult": elo_weight_mult, "ppa_weight_mult": ppa_weight_mult, "advanced_weight_mult": advanced_weight_mult, "tempo_weight_mult": tempo_weight_mult, "spread_ap_min_edge": spread_ap_min_edge, "spread_ap_max_edge": spread_ap_max_edge, "spread_ap_min_agree": spread_ap_min_agree, "spread_ap_max_agree": spread_ap_max_agree, "spread_a_min_edge": spread_a_min_edge, "spread_a_min_agree": spread_a_min_agree, "spread_a_alt_edge": spread_a_alt_edge, "spread_a_alt_agree": spread_a_alt_agree, "spread_b_min_edge": spread_b_min_edge, "spread_b_min_agree": spread_b_min_agree, "spread_late_max_edge": spread_late_max_edge, "ou_ap_min_edge": ou_ap_min_edge, "ou_a_min_edge": ou_a_min_edge, "ou_b_min_edge": ou_b_min_edge, "ml_ap_edge": ml_ap_edge, "ml_ap_min_implied": ml_ap_min_implied, "ml_ap_max_implied": ml_ap_max_implied, "ml_ap_min_agree": ml_ap_min_agree, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, } return backtest_ensemble_tunable(seasons=seasons_list, cfg=cfg) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # PER-MODEL WEEKLY ACCURACY — for re-deriving phase boundaries and weights # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/per-model-by-week") def per_model_by_week( seasons: str = "2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Backtests each individual model's spread prediction by week, season, using look-ahead-free data (weekly advanced stats, prior-season fallback). Returns a matrix: season → week → {model: ats_pct, games, mae}. This is what we need to re-derive phase boundaries (when does each model start to be reliable?) and re-derive phase weights (which model is sharpest in each phase?). use_opening_line=true: use opening lines (matches real-world picks) use_opening_line=false: use closing lines (most informed view) """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.elo_model import predict_elo_from_data, load_elo_data from models.ppa_model import predict_ppa_from_data, load_ppa_game_data, load_ppa_season_data from models.advanced_model import predict_advanced_from_data, load_advanced_stats, load_advanced_stats_weekly from models.ensemble_model import predict_tempo_margin, load_tempo_stats, load_tempo_ppa from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] #
