Load model data sources once sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) elo_data = load_elo_data(all_s) ppa_by_team = load_ppa_game_data(all_s) ppa_seas = load_ppa_season_data(all_s) adv_stats = load_advanced_stats(all_s) adv_weekly = load_advanced_stats_weekly(all_s) tempo_stats = load_tempo_stats(all_s) tempo_ppa_game, tempo_ppa_seas = load_tempo_ppa(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, home_points, away_points, season_type") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, spread, " "opening_spread") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r # Only score games we have results for, in the target seasons games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] # Structure: {(season, week, model): {"games":N, "correct":N, "mae_sum":F}} from collections import defaultdict bucket = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0, "mae_sum": 0.0}) for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season = game["season"] week = game.get("week") ns = game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue # Get line — must have a spread to score ATS ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") if mkt_spread is None: continue actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) # Compute each model's prediction (look-ahead-free) sp_pred = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) elo_pred = predict_elo_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, elo_data) ppa_pred = predict_ppa_from_data(ht, at, season, week, ns, ppa_by_team, ppa_seas) adv_pred = predict_advanced_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, adv_stats, week=week, weekly_idx=adv_weekly) tempo_margin = predict_tempo_margin(ht, at, season, week, ns, tempo_stats, tempo_ppa_game, tempo_ppa_seas) model_preds = { "sp": sp_pred["predicted_margin"] if sp_pred else None, "elo": elo_pred["predicted_margin"] if elo_pred else None, "ppa": ppa_pred["predicted_margin"] if ppa_pred else None, "advanced": adv_pred["predicted_margin"] if adv_pred else None, "tempo": tempo_margin, } # Score each model: predicted spread = -predicted_margin # ATS hit if our pick covers for model_name, pm in model_preds.items(): if pm is None: continue key = (season, week, model_name) bucket[key]["games"] += 1 bucket[key]["mae_sum"] += abs(pm - actual_margin) pred_spread = -pm # We pick home if our spread < market spread pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered if hit: bucket[key]["correct"] += 1 # Reshape into nested dict out = {} for (season, week, model), stats in bucket.items(): out.setdefault(season, {}).setdefault(week, {})[model] = { "games": stats["games"], "correct": stats["correct"], "pct": round(stats["correct"] / stats["games"] * 100, 1) if stats["games"] else 0, "mae": round(stats["mae_sum"] / stats["games"], 2) if stats["games"] else 0, } # Add phase-aggregated rollups for easier consumption # Phase boundaries: 1-5 early, 6-9 mid, 10+ late phase_rollup = {} for season in seasons_list: phase_rollup[season] = {} for phase_name, weeks in [("early_1_5", range(1, 6)), ("mid_6_9", range(6, 10)), ("late_10_plus", range(10, 30))]: agg = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0, "mae_sum": 0.0}) for w in weeks: for (s, ww, model), stats in bucket.items(): if s == season and ww == w: agg[model]["games"] += stats["games"] agg[model]["correct"] += stats["correct"] agg[model]["mae_sum"] += stats["mae_sum"] phase_rollup[season][phase_name] = { model: { "games": data["games"], "correct": data["correct"], "pct": round(data["correct"] / data["games"] * 100, 1) if data["games"] else 0, "mae": round(data["mae_sum"] / data["games"], 2) if data["games"] else 0, } for model, data in agg.items() } # Cross-season phase rollup (all seasons combined by phase) cross_phase = {} for phase_name, weeks in [("early_1_5", range(1, 6)), ("mid_6_9", range(6, 10)), ("late_10_plus", range(10, 30))]: agg = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0, "mae_sum": 0.0}) for w in weeks: for (s, ww, model), stats in bucket.items(): if ww == w: agg[model]["games"] += stats["games"] agg[model]["correct"] += stats["correct"] agg[model]["mae_sum"] += stats["mae_sum"] cross_phase[phase_name] = { model: { "games": data["games"], "correct": data["correct"], "pct": round(data["correct"] / data["games"] * 100, 1) if data["games"] else 0, "mae": round(data["mae_sum"] / data["games"], 2) if data["games"] else 0, } for model, data in agg.items() } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "by_season_week": out, "by_season_phase": phase_rollup, "by_phase": cross_phase, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # SP+ LOSS PATTERN ANALYZER — slice picks by metadata dimensions # to find subsets where SP+ over/underperforms # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/sp-pattern-analyzer") def sp_pattern_analyzer( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Runs SP+-only picks across the requested seasons and slices the results by many metadata dimensions, returning hit rate per bucket. Use this to spot subsets where SP+ is reliably worse than 50% (exclude them) or reliably better than 60% (treat as A+). Slices: - week, phase - is_neutral_site, is_conference_game, is_non_conference - spread_bucket: pickem / -3 / -3to-7 / -7to-14 / -14+ - edge_bucket: how far our pick was from market - sp_picked_favorite vs sp_picked_underdog - sp_picked_home vs sp_picked_away - home_conference, away_conference - total_bucket: low/mid/high game total """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points, " "home_conference, away_conference") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] # Phase mapping def phase_for(w): if w is None: return "unknown" if w <= 5: return "early_1_5" if w <= 9: return "mid_6_9" return "late_10_plus" # Spread bucket — by ABSOLUTE size of market spread def spread_bucket(mkt_spread): if mkt_spread is None: return "unknown" a = abs(mkt_spread) if a < 1.0: return "pickem_lt1" if a <= 3.0: return "small_1to3" if a <= 7.0: return "med_3to7" if a <= 14.0: return "large_7to14" return "huge_14plus" # Edge bucket — how far our prediction was from the market def edge_bucket(edge): if edge is None: return "unknown" if edge < 1.0: return "tiny_lt1" if edge < 2.0: return "small_1to2" if edge < 3.5: return "med_2to3.5" if edge < 6.0: return "big_3.5to6" return "huge_6plus" # Total bucket — game O/U size def total_bucket(total): if total is None: return "unknown" if total < 45: return "very_low_lt45" if total < 52: return "low_45to52" if total < 58: return "mid_52to58" if total < 65: return "high_58to65" return "very_high_65plus" # Each pick records its outcome AND its metadata flags picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("over_under") if mkt_spread is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_spread = -pm actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) # Did SP+ cover? pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered # The market favorite is whoever has the negative spread # If mkt_spread < 0, home is favorite; if > 0, away is favorite market_home_favorite = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_favorite = (pick_home and market_home_favorite) or (not pick_home and not market_home_favorite) edge = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "phase": phase_for(week), "ns": bool(ns), "conf_g": bool(game.get("conference_game", False)), "non_conf": (not game.get("conference_game", False)) and (not ns), "spread_b": spread_bucket(mkt_spread), "edge_b": edge_bucket(edge), "total_b": total_bucket(mkt_total), "sp_picked_home": pick_home, "sp_picked_favorite": sp_picked_favorite, "home_conf": game.get("home_conference"), "away_conf": game.get("away_conference"), "hit": hit, }) if not picks: return {"error": "no picks computed"} total_picks = len(picks) total_correct = sum(1 for p in picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(total_correct / total_picks * 100, 2) # Slice helper def slice_by(key, picks_subset=None): ps = picks_subset if picks_subset is not None else picks buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in ps: k = p.get(key) if isinstance(k, bool): k = "true" if k else "false" if k is None: k = "null" buckets[str(k)]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: buckets[str(k)]["correct"] += 1 return { k: { "games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, } for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()) } by_dimension = { "by_week": slice_by("week"), "by_phase": slice_by("phase"), "by_neutral_site": slice_by("ns"), "by_conference_game": slice_by("conf_g"), "by_non_conf": slice_by("non_conf"), "by_spread_size": slice_by("spread_b"), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b"), "by_total": slice_by("total_b"), "by_sp_picked_home": slice_by("sp_picked_home"), "by_sp_picked_favorite": slice_by("sp_picked_favorite"), "by_home_conference": slice_by("home_conf"), "by_away_conference": slice_by("away_conf"), } # Per-season same slices for cross-checking consistency by_season = {} for s in seasons_list: season_picks = [p for p in picks if p["season"] == s] if not season_picks: continue sc = sum(1 for p in season_picks if p["hit"]) by_season[s] = { "games": len(season_picks), "correct": sc, "pct": round(sc / len(season_picks) * 100, 1), "by_spread_size": slice_by("spread_b", season_picks), "by_phase": slice_by("phase", season_picks), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b", season_picks), "by_sp_picked_favorite": slice_by("sp_picked_favorite", season_picks), } # Cross-dimension: phase × spread_size (to find combo bad spots) phase_spread = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['phase']}__{p['spread_b']}" phase_spread[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: phase_spread[k]["correct"] += 1 phase_spread_out = { k: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for k, v in sorted(phase_spread.items()) } # Phase × favorite-vs-dog phase_fav = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['phase']}__{'fav' if p['sp_picked_favorite'] else 'dog'}" phase_fav[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: phase_fav[k]["correct"] += 1 phase_fav_out = { k: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for k, v in sorted(phase_fav.items()) } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "total_picks": total_picks, "total_correct": total_correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "by_dimension": by_dimension, "by_season": by_season, "cross_phase_spread": phase_spread_out, "cross_phase_favorite": phase_fav_out, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # SMART TIER BACKTEST — uses loss-pattern-derived tier rules # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/backtest-smart-tier") def backtest_smart_tier( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, # Smart-tier rule dials aplus_require_picks_fav: bool = True, aplus_min_edge: float = 1.0, aplus_max_spread: float = 14.0, a_min_edge: float = 3.5, a_max_spread: float = 14.0, b_min_edge: float = 2.0, b_max_edge: float = 3.5, exclude_min_spread: float = 14.0, # auto-C above this market spread exclude_max_edge: float = 1.0, # auto-C below this edge ): """ Backtests SP+-only picks with NEW tier rules derived from the loss-pattern analyzer. Picks where SP+ agrees with market on the favorite hit 75%. Huge spreads (14+) and tiny edges (< 1) are coinflips and excluded. Tier rules (all on absolute spread): EXCLUDE: spread >= 14 OR edge < 1.0 A+: SP+ picks favorite AND spread < 14 AND edge >= 1.0 A: edge >= 3.5 AND spread < 14 (no fav constraint) B: 2.0 <= edge < 3.5 AND spread < 14 C: everything else """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, " "opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] # Tier classifier — three tiers only. # A+ and A are pickable. Everything else is C (no pick). # B was historically a coin flip at 49.7% — including it as a # "tier" implied a recommendation that the data didn't support. def classify_tier(edge, abs_spread, sp_picked_fav): # Hard excludes → no pick if abs_spread >= exclude_min_spread: return "C" if edge < exclude_max_edge: return "C" # A+: agrees with market on favorite, with min edge if (aplus_require_picks_fav and sp_picked_fav and edge >= aplus_min_edge and abs_spread < aplus_max_spread): return "A+" # A: strong edge in reasonable spread range if edge >= a_min_edge and abs_spread < a_max_spread: return "A" # Everything else is "no pick" — don't recommend coin flips return "C" # Collect picks per game with tier classification results = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("away_moneyline") if mkt_spread is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_spread = -pm edge_val = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered # market favorite is the negative side: home if mkt_spread < 0 market_home_fav = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_fav = (pick_home and market_home_fav) or (not pick_home and not market_home_fav) tier = classify_tier(edge_val, abs_spread, sp_picked_fav) results.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "tier": tier, "hit": hit, "sp_picked_fav": sp_picked_fav, "edge": edge_val, "abs_spread": abs_spread, }) if not results: return {"error": "no picks computed"} # Build tier rollup def rollup(items, key="tier"): buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for r in items: k = r[key] buckets[k]["games"] += 1 if r["hit"]: buckets[k]["correct"] += 1 return { k: { "games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, } for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()) } overall_pickable = [r for r in results if r["tier"] != "C"] overall_pct = round( sum(1 for r in overall_pickable if r["hit"]) / len(overall_pickable) * 100, 2 ) if overall_pickable else 0 # Per-season tier breakdown per_season = {} for s in seasons_list: season_items = [r for r in results if r["season"] == s] per_season[s] = { "total_games": len(season_items), "tier_breakdown": rollup(season_items), "pickable_picks": len([r for r in season_items if r["tier"] != "C"]), "per_week_aplus": {}, } # Per-week A+ counts (so we can see picks-per-week) aplus_by_week = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for r in season_items: if r["tier"] == "A+": aplus_by_week[r["week"]]["games"] += 1 if r["hit"]: aplus_by_week[r["week"]]["correct"] += 1 per_season[s]["per_week_aplus"] = { w: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for w, v in sorted(aplus_by_week.items()) } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "rules": { "aplus_require_picks_fav": aplus_require_picks_fav, "aplus_min_edge": aplus_min_edge, "aplus_max_spread": aplus_max_spread, "a_min_edge": a_min_edge, "b_range": [b_min_edge, b_max_edge], "exclude_min_spread": exclude_min_spread, "exclude_max_edge": exclude_max_edge, }, "total_games": len(results), "pickable_picks": len(overall_pickable), "overall_pct": overall_pct, "tier_breakdown": rollup(results), "per_season": per_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # STEP 2: A+ LOSS INSPECTOR # Look at WHICH A+ picks are losing to see if there's a sub-pattern # we can filter to push A+ hit rate even higher. # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/aplus-loss-inspector") def aplus_loss_inspector( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Inspects every A+ pick from the smart-tier system and slices the win/loss outcomes by metadata. Goal: find sub-patterns where A+ is reliably worse, so we can refine the tier. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points, " "home_conference, away_conference") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] def phase_for(w): if w is None: return "unknown" if w <= 5: return "early_1_5" if w <= 9: return "mid_6_9" return "late_10_plus" def spread_bucket(s): a = abs(s) if s is not None else None if a is None: return "unknown" if a < 1.0: return "pickem" if a <= 3.0: return "small_1to3" if a <= 7.0: return "med_3to7" if a <= 14.0: return "large_7to14" return "huge_14plus" def edge_bucket(e): if e is None: return "unknown" if e < 1.0: return "tiny_lt1" if e < 2.0: return "small_1to2" if e < 3.5: return "med_2to3.5" if e < 6.0: return "big_3.5to6" return "huge_6plus" def total_bucket(t): if t is None: return "unknown" if t < 45: return "very_low_lt45" if t < 52: return "low_45to52" if t < 58: return "mid_52to58" if t < 65: return "high_58to65" return "very_high_65plus" # Walk picks, identify A+ ones, score them aplus_picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("over_under") if mkt_spread is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_spread = -pm edge_val = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) # A+ tier filter if abs_spread >= 14.0: continue if edge_val < 1.0: continue pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread market_home_fav = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_fav = (pick_home and market_home_fav) or (not pick_home and not market_home_fav) if not sp_picked_fav: continue # not A+ in our smart tier actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered aplus_picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "phase": phase_for(week), "abs_spread": abs_spread, "edge": edge_val, "spread_b": spread_bucket(mkt_spread), "edge_b": edge_bucket(edge_val), "total_b": total_bucket(mkt_total), "ns": bool(ns), "conf_g": bool(game.get("conference_game", False)), "non_conf": (not game.get("conference_game", False)) and (not ns), "home_conf": game.get("home_conference"), "away_conf": game.get("away_conference"), "pick_home": pick_home, "hit": hit, }) if not aplus_picks: return {"error": "no A+ picks"} total = len(aplus_picks) correct = sum(1 for p in aplus_picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(correct / total * 100, 2) def slice_by(key, subset=None): ps = subset if subset is not None else aplus_picks buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in ps: k = p.get(key) if isinstance(k, bool): k = "true" if k else "false" if k is None: k = "null" buckets[str(k)]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: buckets[str(k)]["correct"] += 1 return { k: { "games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, } for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()) } by_dim = { "by_phase": slice_by("phase"), "by_spread_size": slice_by("spread_b"), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b"), "by_total": slice_by("total_b"), "by_neutral_site": slice_by("ns"), "by_conf_game": slice_by("conf_g"), "by_non_conf": slice_by("non_conf"), "by_home_conference": slice_by("home_conf"), "by_away_conference": slice_by("away_conf"), "by_pick_home": slice_by("pick_home"), } # 2D slices phase_spread = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in aplus_picks: k = f"{p['phase']}__{p['spread_b']}" phase_spread[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: phase_spread[k]["correct"] += 1 spread_edge = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in aplus_picks: k = f"{p['spread_b']}__{p['edge_b']}" spread_edge[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: spread_edge[k]["correct"] += 1 def fmt(d): return {k: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for k, v in sorted(d.items())} return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "total_aplus": total, "correct": correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "by_dimension": by_dim, "cross_phase_spread": fmt(phase_spread), "cross_spread_edge": fmt(spread_edge), } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # POTW BACKTEST — single highest-confidence A+ pick per week # Selects the A+ pick with the largest edge each week and reports # season-by-season record. This is "the bet of the week." # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/backtest-potw") def backtest_potw( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ POTW (Pick of the Week) backtest: for each (season, week), select the single A+ pick with the highest edge and score it. This is the headline "highest confidence game of the week" feature. A+ criteria (matches /admin/backtest-smart-tier defaults): - SP+ picks the favorite (agrees with market) - Edge >= 1.0 - Absolute market spread < 14 """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] # Collect every A+ pick aplus_picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") if mkt_spread is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_spread = -pm edge_val = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) # A+ filter if abs_spread >= 14.0: continue if edge_val < 1.0: continue pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread market_home_fav = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_fav = (pick_home and market_home_fav) or (not pick_home and not market_home_fav) if not sp_picked_fav: continue actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered aplus_picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "home": ht, "away": at, "mkt_spread": mkt_spread, "abs_spread": abs_spread, "edge": edge_val, "pick_home": pick_home, "pick_team": ht if pick_home else at, "pred_margin": pm, "actual_margin": actual_margin, "hit": hit, }) if not aplus_picks: return {"error": "no A+ picks"} # For each (season, week), pick the one with the largest edge by_sw = defaultdict(list) for p in aplus_picks: by_sw[(p["season"], p["week"])].append(p) potw_picks = [] for (season, week), week_picks in sorted(by_sw.items()): best = max(week_picks, key=lambda x: x["edge"]) potw_picks.append(best) # Score total = len(potw_picks) correct = sum(1 for p in potw_picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(correct / total * 100, 2) if total else 0 # Per-season breakdown per_season = {} for s in seasons_list: season_picks = [p for p in potw_picks if p["season"] == s] sc = sum(1 for p in season_picks if p["hit"]) per_season[s] = { "weeks": len(season_picks), "wins": sc, "losses": len(season_picks) - sc, "pct": round(sc / len(season_picks) * 100, 1) if season_picks else 0, "picks": [ { "week": p["week"], "pick": p["pick_team"], "vs": (p["away"] if p["pick_home"] else p["home"]), "spread": p["mkt_spread"] if p["pick_home"] else -p["mkt_spread"], "edge": round(p["edge"], 1), "actual": p["actual_margin"] if p["pick_home"] else -p["actual_margin"], "hit": p["hit"], } for p in season_picks ], } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "method": "Pick the A+ game with the largest edge each week", "total_weeks": total, "wins": correct, "losses": total - correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "per_season": per_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # OU PATTERN ANALYZER — slice O/U picks by metadata # Looking for sub-patterns where the model is most reliable on totals. # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/ou-pattern-analyzer") def ou_pattern_analyzer( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Runs SP+-only O/U picks across the requested seasons and slices the results by many metadata dimensions, returning hit rate per bucket. For each game we compute SP+'s predicted total (just sum the two team SP+ averages — predict_sp_from_data already returns predicted_total). We pick OVER if predicted > market, UNDER otherwise. Slices include the same dims as spread analyzer plus: - over_or_under: did we pick over or under - market_total_bucket: 45-, 45-52, 52-58, 58-65, 65+ - edge_bucket: how far our prediction was from market """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points, " "home_conference, away_conference") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] def phase_for(w): if w is None: return "unknown" if w <= 5: return "early_1_5" if w <= 9: return "mid_6_9" return "late_10_plus" def total_bucket(t): if t is None: return "unknown" if t < 45: return "very_low_lt45" if t < 52: return "low_45to52" if t < 58: return "mid_52to58" if t < 65: return "high_58to65" return "very_high_65plus" def edge_bucket(e): if e is None: return "unknown" if e < 1.0: return "tiny_lt1" if e < 2.0: return "small_1to2" if e < 4.0: return "med_2to4" if e < 7.0: return "big_4to7" return "huge_7plus" def spread_bucket(s): a = abs(s) if s is not None else None if a is None: return "unknown" if a < 1.0: return "pickem" if a <= 3.0: return "small_1to3" if a <= 7.0: return "med_3to7" if a <= 14.0: return "large_7to14" return "huge_14plus" picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") else: mkt_total = line.get("over_under") mkt_spread = line.get("spread") if mkt_total is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pred_total = sp.get("predicted_total") if pred_total is None: continue edge_val = abs(pred_total - mkt_total) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) # Pick over if predicted > market pick_over = pred_total > mkt_total # Hit if actual total agrees with our pick hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) # Push doesn't really happen on totals with decimal lines; if it does count as miss if actual_total == mkt_total: continue picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "phase": phase_for(week), "ns": bool(ns), "conf_g": bool(game.get("conference_game", False)), "non_conf": (not game.get("conference_game", False)) and (not ns), "total_b": total_bucket(mkt_total), "edge_b": edge_bucket(edge_val), "spread_b": spread_bucket(mkt_spread), "over_under": "over" if pick_over else "under", "home_conf": game.get("home_conference"), "away_conf": game.get("away_conference"), "hit": hit, }) if not picks: return {"error": "no picks"} total = len(picks) correct = sum(1 for p in picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(correct / total * 100, 2) def slice_by(key, subset=None): ps = subset if subset is not None else picks buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in ps: k = p.get(key) if isinstance(k, bool): k = "true" if k else "false" if k is None: k = "null" buckets[str(k)]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: buckets[str(k)]["correct"] += 1 return { k: { "games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, } for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()) } by_dim = { "by_week": slice_by("week"), "by_phase": slice_by("phase"), "by_neutral_site": slice_by("ns"), "by_conf_game": slice_by("conf_g"), "by_non_conf": slice_by("non_conf"), "by_total": slice_by("total_b"), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b"), "by_spread": slice_by("spread_b"), "by_over_under": slice_by("over_under"), "by_home_conf": slice_by("home_conf"), "by_away_conf": slice_by("away_conf"), } # 2D slices total_edge = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['total_b']}__{p['edge_b']}" total_edge[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: total_edge[k]["correct"] += 1 total_over_under = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['total_b']}__{p['over_under']}" total_over_under[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: total_over_under[k]["correct"] += 1 edge_over_under = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['edge_b']}__{p['over_under']}" edge_over_under[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: edge_over_under[k]["correct"] += 1 def fmt(d): return {k: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for k, v in sorted(d.items())} # Per season slice by_season = {} for s in seasons_list: sp_subset = [p for p in picks if p["season"] == s] if not sp_subset: continue sc = sum(1 for p in sp_subset if p["hit"]) by_season[s] = { "games": len(sp_subset), "correct": sc, "pct": round(sc / len(sp_subset) * 100, 1), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b", sp_subset), "by_total": slice_by("total_b", sp_subset), "by_over_under": slice_by("over_under", sp_subset), } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "total_picks": total, "total_correct": correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "by_dimension": by_dim, "cross_total_edge": fmt(total_edge), "cross_total_over_under": fmt(total_over_under), "cross_edge_over_under": fmt(edge_over_under), "by_season": by_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # ML PATTERN ANALYZER — slice ML picks by metadata # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/ml-pattern-analyzer") def ml_pattern_analyzer( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, ): """ Runs SP+-only ML picks across the requested seasons and slices results by metadata dimensions to find ML A+ rules. For each game we use SP+'s predicted_margin to derive a win probability, compare to the market implied win probability (no-vig), and pick whichever side has more edge. Slices include the same dims as spread analyzer plus: - implied_prob_bucket (favorite-heavy, pickem, dog-heavy) - edge_bucket (probability edge size) - sp_picked_home, sp_picked_favorite """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.ensemble_model import no_vig_prob from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points, " "home_conference, away_conference") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, " "opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] def phase_for(w): if w is None: return "unknown" if w <= 5: return "early_1_5" if w <= 9: return "mid_6_9" return "late_10_plus" def implied_bucket(impl): if impl is None: return "unknown" if impl < 0.25: return "deep_dog_lt25" if impl < 0.40: return "dog_25to40" if impl < 0.55: return "pickem_40to55" if impl < 0.70: return "fav_55to70" return "heavy_fav_gt70" def edge_bucket(e): # probability edge, 0-1 scale if e is None: return "unknown" if e < 0.05: return "tiny_lt05" if e < 0.10: return "small_05to10" if e < 0.15: return "med_10to15" if e < 0.20: return "big_15to20" return "huge_20plus" def spread_bucket(s): a = abs(s) if s is not None else None if a is None: return "unknown" if a < 1.0: return "pickem" if a <= 3.0: return "small_1to3" if a <= 7.0: return "med_3to7" if a <= 14.0: return "large_7to14" return "huge_14plus" picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") home_ml = line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") home_ml = line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("away_moneyline") if home_ml is None or away_ml is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue sp_win_prob_home = sp.get("win_prob_home") if sp_win_prob_home is None: continue home_implied, away_implied = no_vig_prob(home_ml, away_ml) if home_implied is None: continue # Compute edges for both sides; pick whichever is bigger and positive home_edge = sp_win_prob_home - home_implied away_edge = (1 - sp_win_prob_home) - away_implied if home_edge >= away_edge and home_edge > 0: pick_side = "home" pick_edge = home_edge pick_implied = home_implied elif away_edge > 0: pick_side = "away" pick_edge = away_edge pick_implied = away_implied else: continue # no edge on either side, skip actual_home_win = (game["home_points"] or 0) > (game["away_points"] or 0) hit = (pick_side == "home") == actual_home_win # Did we pick the favorite (lower moneyline = favorite)? if pick_side == "home": we_picked_fav = home_ml < away_ml else: we_picked_fav = away_ml < home_ml picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "phase": phase_for(week), "ns": bool(ns), "conf_g": bool(game.get("conference_game", False)), "non_conf": (not game.get("conference_game", False)) and (not ns), "implied_b": implied_bucket(pick_implied), "edge_b": edge_bucket(pick_edge), "spread_b": spread_bucket(mkt_spread), "pick_side": pick_side, "pick_fav": we_picked_fav, "home_conf": game.get("home_conference"), "away_conf": game.get("away_conference"), "hit": hit, }) if not picks: return {"error": "no picks"} total = len(picks) correct = sum(1 for p in picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(correct / total * 100, 2) def slice_by(key, subset=None): ps = subset if subset is not None else picks buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in ps: k = p.get(key) if isinstance(k, bool): k = "true" if k else "false" if k is None: k = "null" buckets[str(k)]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: buckets[str(k)]["correct"] += 1 return { k: { "games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, } for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()) } by_dim = { "by_week": slice_by("week"), "by_phase": slice_by("phase"), "by_neutral_site": slice_by("ns"), "by_conf_game": slice_by("conf_g"), "by_non_conf": slice_by("non_conf"), "by_implied": slice_by("implied_b"), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b"), "by_spread": slice_by("spread_b"), "by_pick_side": slice_by("pick_side"), "by_pick_favorite": slice_by("pick_fav"), "by_home_conf": slice_by("home_conf"), "by_away_conf": slice_by("away_conf"), } # 2D slices impl_edge = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['implied_b']}__{p['edge_b']}" impl_edge[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: impl_edge[k]["correct"] += 1 impl_pickside = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['implied_b']}__{'fav' if p['pick_fav'] else 'dog'}" impl_pickside[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: impl_pickside[k]["correct"] += 1 edge_pickside = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "correct": 0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['edge_b']}__{'fav' if p['pick_fav'] else 'dog'}" edge_pickside[k]["games"] += 1 if p["hit"]: edge_pickside[k]["correct"] += 1 def fmt(d): return {k: {"games": v["games"], "correct": v["correct"], "pct": round(v["correct"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0} for k, v in sorted(d.items())} # Per season by_season = {} for s in seasons_list: sp_subset = [p for p in picks if p["season"] == s] if not sp_subset: continue sc = sum(1 for p in sp_subset if p["hit"]) by_season[s] = { "games": len(sp_subset), "correct": sc, "pct": round(sc / len(sp_subset) * 100, 1), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b", sp_subset), "by_implied": slice_by("implied_b", sp_subset), "by_pick_favorite": slice_by("pick_fav", sp_subset), } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "total_picks": total, "total_correct": correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "by_dimension": by_dim, "cross_implied_edge": fmt(impl_edge), "cross_implied_pickside": fmt(impl_pickside), "cross_edge_pickside": fmt(edge_pickside), "by_season": by_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # ML ROI ANALYZER — slice ML picks by metadata WITH ROI/profit # This is the right way to evaluate ML picks. Hit rate alone is # misleading because payouts vary wildly. We compute profit on # $100 flat bets using actual moneyline odds. # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/ml-roi-analyzer") def ml_roi_analyzer( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, bet_size: float = 100.0, ): """ Same as ml_pattern_analyzer but reports ROI/profit per bucket. For a winning pick at moneyline `ml`: payout = bet_size * (100/abs(ml)) if ml < 0 else bet_size * (ml/100) For a loss: -bet_size Each bucket reports: - games, wins, losses - hit_pct - total_bet (games * bet_size) - total_profit (sum of payouts on wins minus losses) - roi_pct (total_profit / total_bet * 100) """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.ensemble_model import no_vig_prob from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, " "opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] def implied_bucket(impl): if impl is None: return "unknown" if impl < 0.25: return "deep_dog_lt25" if impl < 0.40: return "dog_25to40" if impl < 0.55: return "pickem_40to55" if impl < 0.70: return "fav_55to70" return "heavy_fav_gt70" def edge_bucket(e): if e is None: return "unknown" if e < 0.05: return "tiny_lt05" if e < 0.10: return "small_05to10" if e < 0.15: return "med_10to15" if e < 0.20: return "big_15to20" return "huge_20plus" def ml_bucket(ml): # The price you're getting; helps identify "value dog" pockets if ml is None: return "unknown" if ml <= -300: return "heavy_chalk_lt-300" if ml <= -150: return "chalk_-150_to_-300" if ml <= 100: return "near_pickem_-150_to_+100" if ml <= 200: return "small_dog_+100_to_+200" if ml <= 350: return "big_dog_+200_to_+350" return "huge_dog_gt_+350" def payout(ml, won, bet): if not won: return -bet if ml < 0: return bet * (100 / abs(ml)) else: return bet * (ml / 100) picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: home_ml = line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline") mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") else: home_ml = line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("away_moneyline") mkt_spread = line.get("spread") if home_ml is None or away_ml is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue sp_win_prob_home = sp.get("win_prob_home") if sp_win_prob_home is None: continue home_implied, away_implied = no_vig_prob(home_ml, away_ml) if home_implied is None: continue home_edge = sp_win_prob_home - home_implied away_edge = (1 - sp_win_prob_home) - away_implied if home_edge >= away_edge and home_edge > 0: pick_side = "home" pick_edge = home_edge pick_implied = home_implied pick_ml = home_ml elif away_edge > 0: pick_side = "away" pick_edge = away_edge pick_implied = away_implied pick_ml = away_ml else: continue actual_home_win = (game["home_points"] or 0) > (game["away_points"] or 0) won = (pick_side == "home") == actual_home_win # Did we pick the favorite (lower ML)? if pick_side == "home": we_picked_fav = home_ml < away_ml else: we_picked_fav = away_ml < home_ml profit = payout(pick_ml, won, bet_size) picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "implied_b": implied_bucket(pick_implied), "edge_b": edge_bucket(pick_edge), "ml_b": ml_bucket(pick_ml), "pick_side": pick_side, "pick_fav": we_picked_fav, "pick_ml": pick_ml, "won": won, "profit": profit, }) if not picks: return {"error": "no picks"} total = len(picks) wins = sum(1 for p in picks if p["won"]) total_bet = total * bet_size total_profit = sum(p["profit"] for p in picks) overall_pct = round(wins / total * 100, 2) overall_roi = round(total_profit / total_bet * 100, 2) def slice_by(key, subset=None): ps = subset if subset is not None else picks buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "wins": 0, "profit": 0.0}) for p in ps: k = p.get(key) if isinstance(k, bool): k = "true" if k else "false" if k is None: k = "null" buckets[str(k)]["games"] += 1 buckets[str(k)]["profit"] += p["profit"] if p["won"]: buckets[str(k)]["wins"] += 1 out = {} for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()): bet_total = v["games"] * bet_size out[k] = { "games": v["games"], "wins": v["wins"], "losses": v["games"] - v["wins"], "hit_pct": round(v["wins"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, "total_bet": round(bet_total, 2), "profit": round(v["profit"], 2), "roi_pct": round(v["profit"] / bet_total * 100, 2) if bet_total else 0, } return out by_dim = { "by_implied": slice_by("implied_b"), "by_edge": slice_by("edge_b"), "by_ml_price": slice_by("ml_b"), "by_pick_favorite": slice_by("pick_fav"), "by_pick_side": slice_by("pick_side"), } # 2D slices — most important here impl_edge = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "wins": 0, "profit": 0.0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['implied_b']}__{p['edge_b']}" impl_edge[k]["games"] += 1 impl_edge[k]["profit"] += p["profit"] if p["won"]: impl_edge[k]["wins"] += 1 ml_edge = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "wins": 0, "profit": 0.0}) for p in picks: k = f"{p['ml_b']}__{p['edge_b']}" ml_edge[k]["games"] += 1 ml_edge[k]["profit"] += p["profit"] if p["won"]: ml_edge[k]["wins"] += 1 def fmt(d): out = {} for k, v in sorted(d.items()): bet_total = v["games"] * bet_size out[k] = { "games": v["games"], "wins": v["wins"], "hit_pct": round(v["wins"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, "profit": round(v["profit"], 2), "roi_pct": round(v["profit"] / bet_total * 100, 2) if bet_total else 0, } return out # Per season by_season = {} for s in seasons_list: ss = [p for p in picks if p["season"] == s] if not ss: continue sw = sum(1 for p in ss if p["won"]) sp_prof = sum(p["profit"] for p in ss) bet_total = len(ss) * bet_size by_season[s] = { "games": len(ss), "wins": sw, "hit_pct": round(sw / len(ss) * 100, 1), "profit": round(sp_prof, 2), "roi_pct": round(sp_prof / bet_total * 100, 2), "by_implied": slice_by("implied_b", ss), "by_ml_price": slice_by("ml_b", ss), "by_pick_favorite": slice_by("pick_fav", ss), } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "bet_size": bet_size, "total_picks": total, "total_wins": wins, "total_bet": round(total_bet, 2), "total_profit": round(total_profit, 2), "overall_hit_pct": overall_pct, "overall_roi_pct": overall_roi, "by_dimension": by_dim, "cross_implied_edge": fmt(impl_edge), "cross_ml_price_edge": fmt(ml_edge), "by_season": by_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # UNIFIED SMART-TIER BACKTEST — the product-defining endpoint # Classifies every game across spread/OU/ML, picks weekly headlines: # - POTW (best A+ from spread + OU by edge) # - Smart Money ML (highest hit-rate +EV ML) # - Lottery Shot ML (highest expected payout +EV ML) # - POTW Parlay (top 3 A+ spread+OU by edge, 3-leg parlay) # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/backtest-unified") def backtest_unified( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, # Spread tier rules spread_aplus_max_spread: float = 14.0, spread_aplus_min_edge: float = 1.0, spread_a_min_edge: float = 3.5, spread_a_max_spread: float = 14.0, # OU tier rules ou_aplus_min_edge: float = 7.0, ou_aplus_max_total: float = 65.0, ou_a_min_edge: float = 4.0, ou_a_max_total: float = 65.0, # ML — Smart Money rules (high hit, +EV) sm_min_edge: float = 0.10, sm_min_ml: float = -300.0, sm_max_ml: float = 200.0, # ML — Lottery Shot rules (big payout, +EV) ls_min_edge: float = 0.15, ls_min_ml: float = 150.0, # Parlay parlay_legs: int = 3, parlay_payout_multiplier: float = 6.0, # ~3-leg -110 parlay pays ~6:1 ): """ Unified product-defining backtest. Returns per-season records for the full PressBox product lineup: weekly POTW, Smart Money ML, Lottery Shot ML, POTW Parlay, plus the A+/A tier listings across all 3 bet types. """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.ensemble_model import no_vig_prob from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, " "opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] def payout_of(ml, won, bet=100): if not won: return -bet if ml < 0: return bet * (100 / abs(ml)) else: return bet * (ml / 100) # Build picks list per game with all 3 bet types' classifications picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("away_moneyline") sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_total = sp.get("predicted_total") sp_win_prob_home = sp.get("win_prob_home") pick = { "season": season, "week": week, "home": ht, "away": at, "spread_pick": None, "spread_tier": None, "spread_hit": None, "spread_edge": None, "ou_pick": None, "ou_tier": None, "ou_hit": None, "ou_edge": None, "ml_pick": None, "ml_tier": None, "ml_hit": None, "ml_edge": None, "ml_implied": None, "ml_price": None, "ml_payout": None, } actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_home_win = actual_margin > 0 # ───── SPREAD ───── if mkt_spread is not None: pred_spread = -pm edge_val = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread market_home_fav = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_fav = (pick_home and market_home_fav) or (not pick_home and not market_home_fav) home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered # Tier classification tier = None if abs_spread < 14 and edge_val >= 1: if sp_picked_fav and abs_spread < spread_aplus_max_spread and edge_val >= spread_aplus_min_edge: tier = "A+" elif edge_val >= spread_a_min_edge and abs_spread < spread_a_max_spread: tier = "A" pick["spread_pick"] = ht if pick_home else at pick["spread_tier"] = tier pick["spread_hit"] = hit pick["spread_edge"] = edge_val pick["spread_mkt"] = mkt_spread # ───── OVER/UNDER ───── if mkt_total is not None and pred_total is not None: edge_val = abs(pred_total - mkt_total) pick_over = pred_total > mkt_total hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) if actual_total == mkt_total: hit = None tier = None if mkt_total < ou_aplus_max_total and edge_val >= ou_aplus_min_edge: tier = "A+" elif mkt_total < ou_a_max_total and edge_val >= ou_a_min_edge: tier = "A" pick["ou_pick"] = "over" if pick_over else "under" pick["ou_tier"] = tier pick["ou_hit"] = hit pick["ou_edge"] = edge_val pick["ou_mkt"] = mkt_total # ───── MONEYLINE ───── if home_ml is not None and away_ml is not None and sp_win_prob_home is not None: home_implied, away_implied = no_vig_prob(home_ml, away_ml) if home_implied is not None: he = sp_win_prob_home - home_implied ae = (1 - sp_win_prob_home) - away_implied if he >= ae and he > 0: side = "home"; ml_edge = he; ml_impl = home_implied; ml_price = home_ml elif ae > 0: side = "away"; ml_edge = ae; ml_impl = away_implied; ml_price = away_ml else: side = None if side: ml_hit = (side == "home") == actual_home_win ml_payout = payout_of(ml_price, ml_hit, 100) # Tier classification ml_tier = None # Smart Money: high hit + +EV if (ml_edge >= sm_min_edge and sm_min_ml <= ml_price <= sm_max_ml): ml_tier = "smart_money" # Lottery Shot: big payout + +EV (overrides smart money on # priced dogs we'd label SM if range overlapped) if (ml_edge >= ls_min_edge and ml_price >= ls_min_ml): ml_tier = "lottery_shot" pick["ml_pick"] = ht if side == "home" else at pick["ml_tier"] = ml_tier pick["ml_hit"] = ml_hit pick["ml_edge"] = ml_edge pick["ml_implied"] = ml_impl pick["ml_price"] = ml_price pick["ml_payout"] = ml_payout picks.append(pick) # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # TIER ROLLUPS # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── def tier_rollup(items, tier_key, hit_key, payout_key=None): buckets = defaultdict(lambda: {"games": 0, "wins": 0, "profit": 0.0}) for p in items: t = p[tier_key] if t is None: continue buckets[t]["games"] += 1 if p[hit_key] == True: buckets[t]["wins"] += 1 if payout_key and p[hit_key] is not None: buckets[t]["profit"] += p.get(payout_key, 0) or 0 elif p[hit_key] == True: # For non-ML bets we count $90.91 win on $100 bet at -110 odds buckets[t]["profit"] += 90.91 elif p[hit_key] == False: buckets[t]["profit"] -= 100 out = {} for k, v in sorted(buckets.items()): bet_total = v["games"] * 100 out[k] = { "games": v["games"], "wins": v["wins"], "losses": v["games"] - v["wins"], "hit_pct": round(v["wins"] / v["games"] * 100, 1) if v["games"] else 0, "profit": round(v["profit"], 2), "roi_pct": round(v["profit"] / bet_total * 100, 2) if bet_total else 0, } return out # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # WEEKLY HEADLINE PICK SELECTION # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── def select_potw(week_picks): """Single best A+ pick from spread + OU combined, by edge.""" candidates = [] for p in week_picks: if p["spread_tier"] == "A+": candidates.append({ "bet_type": "spread", "edge": p["spread_edge"], "team": p["spread_pick"], "vs": p["away"] if p["spread_pick"] == p["home"] else p["home"], "line": p.get("spread_mkt"), "hit": p["spread_hit"], }) if p["ou_tier"] == "A+": candidates.append({ "bet_type": "ou", "edge": p["ou_edge"], "pick": p["ou_pick"], "matchup": f"{p['away']} @ {p['home']}", "total": p.get("ou_mkt"), "hit": p["ou_hit"], }) if not candidates: return None return max(candidates, key=lambda c: c["edge"]) def select_smart_money(week_picks): """Highest hit-rate confidence Smart Money ML pick. We don't know future hit rate per game so we use ml_implied as proxy for confidence: higher implied = higher historical hit rate.""" cands = [p for p in week_picks if p["ml_tier"] == "smart_money"] if not cands: return None best = max(cands, key=lambda p: p["ml_implied"]) return { "team": best["ml_pick"], "matchup": f"{best['away']} @ {best['home']}", "ml": best["ml_price"], "edge": best["ml_edge"], "implied": best["ml_implied"], "hit": best["ml_hit"], "profit": best["ml_payout"], } def select_lottery_shot(week_picks): """Highest expected dollar EV among Lottery Shot picks. EV = (ml_edge_implied_winprob * payout) - ((1 - p) * 100) We use implied win prob from our edge + market implied as our prob estimate.""" cands = [p for p in week_picks if p["ml_tier"] == "lottery_shot"] if not cands: return None def ev(p): our_prob = p["ml_implied"] + p["ml_edge"] # our estimated prob of winning if p["ml_price"] < 0: win_amt = 100 * (100 / abs(p["ml_price"])) else: win_amt = 100 * (p["ml_price"] / 100) return our_prob * win_amt - (1 - our_prob) * 100 best = max(cands, key=ev) return { "team": best["ml_pick"], "matchup": f"{best['away']} @ {best['home']}", "ml": best["ml_price"], "edge": best["ml_edge"], "implied": best["ml_implied"], "expected_value": round(ev(best), 2), "hit": best["ml_hit"], "profit": best["ml_payout"], } def select_parlay(week_picks): """Top 3 A+ from spread + OU combined by edge.""" candidates = [] for p in week_picks: if p["spread_tier"] == "A+": candidates.append({ "bet_type": "spread", "edge": p["spread_edge"], "pick": p["spread_pick"], "hit": p["spread_hit"], }) if p["ou_tier"] == "A+": candidates.append({ "bet_type": "ou", "edge": p["ou_edge"], "pick": f"{p['ou_pick']} {p.get('ou_mkt')}", "hit": p["ou_hit"], }) if len(candidates) < parlay_legs: return None chosen = sorted(candidates, key=lambda c: -c["edge"])[:parlay_legs] all_hit = all(c["hit"] == True for c in chosen) return { "legs": chosen, "hit": all_hit, "payout": round(100 * parlay_payout_multiplier - 100, 2) if all_hit else -100, } # Group picks by (season, week) by_sw = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: by_sw[(p["season"], p["week"])].append(p) # Run through each week to assemble headline picks potw_results = [] smart_money_results = [] lottery_shot_results = [] parlay_results = [] for (season, week), week_picks in sorted(by_sw.items()): potw = select_potw(week_picks) if potw: potw["season"] = season; potw["week"] = week; potw_results.append(potw) sm = select_smart_money(week_picks) if sm: sm["season"] = season; sm["week"] = week; smart_money_results.append(sm) ls = select_lottery_shot(week_picks) if ls: ls["season"] = season; ls["week"] = week; lottery_shot_results.append(ls) parlay = select_parlay(week_picks) if parlay: parlay["season"] = season; parlay["week"] = week; parlay_results.append(parlay) # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # Headline product summaries # ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── def summarize_potw(results): wins = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == True) losses = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == False) total = wins + losses return { "weeks_with_pick": len(results), "wins": wins, "losses": losses, "hit_pct": round(wins / total * 100, 1) if total else 0, "profit_at_100": round(wins * 90.91 - losses * 100, 2), } def summarize_ml(results): wins = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == True) losses = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == False) total = wins + losses profit = sum(r["profit"] for r in results if r.get("profit") is not None) return { "weeks_with_pick": len(results), "wins": wins, "losses": losses, "hit_pct": round(wins / total * 100, 1) if total else 0, "profit_at_100": round(profit, 2), "roi_pct": round(profit / (total * 100) * 100, 2) if total else 0, } def summarize_parlay(results): wins = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == True) losses = sum(1 for r in results if r["hit"] == False) total = wins + losses profit = sum(r["payout"] for r in results) return { "weeks_with_pick": len(results), "wins": wins, "losses": losses, "hit_pct": round(wins / total * 100, 1) if total else 0, "profit_at_100": round(profit, 2), "roi_pct": round(profit / (total * 100) * 100, 2) if total else 0, } # Per-season breakdown of headline products per_season_summary = {} for s in seasons_list: per_season_summary[s] = { "potw": summarize_potw([r for r in potw_results if r["season"] == s]), "smart_money": summarize_ml([r for r in smart_money_results if r["season"] == s]), "lottery_shot": summarize_ml([r for r in lottery_shot_results if r["season"] == s]), "parlay": summarize_parlay([r for r in parlay_results if r["season"] == s]), "tiers": { "spread": tier_rollup([p for p in picks if p["season"] == s], "spread_tier", "spread_hit"), "ou": tier_rollup([p for p in picks if p["season"] == s], "ou_tier", "ou_hit"), "ml": tier_rollup([p for p in picks if p["season"] == s], "ml_tier", "ml_hit", payout_key="ml_payout"), }, } # Aggregate (all seasons) return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "config": { "spread_aplus": {"max_spread": spread_aplus_max_spread, "min_edge": spread_aplus_min_edge}, "ou_aplus": {"min_edge": ou_aplus_min_edge, "max_total": ou_aplus_max_total}, "smart_money": {"min_edge": sm_min_edge, "ml_range": [sm_min_ml, sm_max_ml]}, "lottery_shot": {"min_edge": ls_min_edge, "min_ml": ls_min_ml}, "parlay_legs": parlay_legs, "parlay_payout_x": parlay_payout_multiplier, }, "headline_products": { "potw": summarize_potw(potw_results), "smart_money": summarize_ml(smart_money_results), "lottery_shot": summarize_ml(lottery_shot_results), "parlay": summarize_parlay(parlay_results), }, "tier_breakdowns_all_seasons": { "spread": tier_rollup(picks, "spread_tier", "spread_hit"), "ou": tier_rollup(picks, "ou_tier", "ou_hit"), "ml": tier_rollup(picks, "ml_tier", "ml_hit", payout_key="ml_payout"), }, "per_season": per_season_summary, "weekly_picks": { "potw": potw_results, "smart_money": smart_money_results, "lottery_shot": lottery_shot_results, "parlay": parlay_results, }, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # TOTAL OF THE WEEK BACKTEST — single highest-edge A+ O/U pick per week # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── @app.get("/admin/backtest-totw") def backtest_totw( seasons: str = "2022,2023,2024,2025", use_opening_line: bool = True, aplus_min_edge: float = 7.0, aplus_max_total: float = 65.0, ): """ Total of the Week backtest: for each (season, week), select the single A+ O/U pick with the highest edge and score it. A+ O/U criteria (matches /admin/backtest-unified defaults): - Edge >= 7.0 - Market total < 65.0 """ import traceback try: from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from collections import defaultdict from pipeline.db import get_db seasons_list = [int(s.strip()) for s in seasons.split(",") if s.strip()] all_s = seasons_list + [min(seasons_list) - 1] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() all_games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, home_points, away_points") .in_("season", all_s) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "over_under, opening_over_under") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null") ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in all_games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None and g.get("season") in seasons_list] aplus_picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] season, week, ns = game["season"], game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") else: mkt_total = line.get("over_under") if mkt_total is None: continue sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pred_total = sp.get("predicted_total") if pred_total is None: continue edge_val = abs(pred_total - mkt_total) pick_over = pred_total > mkt_total # A+ filter if mkt_total >= aplus_max_total: continue if edge_val < aplus_min_edge: continue actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) if actual_total == mkt_total: continue hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) aplus_picks.append({ "season": season, "week": week, "home": ht, "away": at, "mkt_total": mkt_total, "pred_total": pred_total, "edge": edge_val, "pick": "over" if pick_over else "under", "actual_total": actual_total, "hit": hit, }) if not aplus_picks: return {"error": "no A+ O/U picks"} # For each (season, week), pick the one with the largest edge by_sw = defaultdict(list) for p in aplus_picks: by_sw[(p["season"], p["week"])].append(p) totw_picks = [] for (season, week), week_picks in sorted(by_sw.items()): best = max(week_picks, key=lambda x: x["edge"]) totw_picks.append(best) total = len(totw_picks) correct = sum(1 for p in totw_picks if p["hit"]) overall_pct = round(correct / total * 100, 2) if total else 0 per_season = {} for s in seasons_list: season_picks = [p for p in totw_picks if p["season"] == s] sc = sum(1 for p in season_picks if p["hit"]) per_season[s] = { "weeks": len(season_picks), "wins": sc, "losses": len(season_picks) - sc, "pct": round(sc / len(season_picks) * 100, 1) if season_picks else 0, "picks": [ { "week": p["week"], "pick": f"{p['pick']} {p['mkt_total']}", "matchup": f"{p['away']} @ {p['home']}", "edge": round(p["edge"], 1), "actual_total": p["actual_total"], "hit": p["hit"], } for p in season_picks ], } return { "seasons": seasons_list, "use_opening_line": use_opening_line, "method": "Pick the A+ O/U game with the largest edge each week", "total_weeks": total, "wins": correct, "losses": total - correct, "overall_pct": overall_pct, "per_season": per_season, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── # RESULTS PAGE ENDPOINTS — public-facing, per-season, per-product # Returns data in the shape the frontend already renders. # ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── def _build_results_picks(season: int, use_opening_line: bool = True): """ Helper: walks all games in a season, returns a list of pick dicts with full metadata for spread, OU, and ML, scored against actual results. """ from models.sp_model import predict_sp_from_data, load_all_sp_ratings from models.ensemble_model import no_vig_prob from pipeline.db import get_db all_s = [season - 1, season] sp_ratings = load_all_sp_ratings(all_s) db = get_db() games_raw = fetch_all( db.table("games") .select("id, home_team, away_team, season, week, " "neutral_site, conference_game, " "home_points, away_points, " "home_conference, away_conference") .eq("season", season) ) lines_raw = fetch_all( db.table("betting_lines") .select("home_team, away_team, season, week, " "spread, opening_spread, over_under, opening_over_under, " "home_moneyline, away_moneyline, " "opening_home_ml, opening_away_ml") .eq("provider", "Bovada").not_.is_("home_team", "null").eq("season", season) ) lines = {} for r in lines_raw: ht = (r.get("home_team") or "").strip().lower() at = (r.get("away_team") or "").strip().lower() s, w = r.get("season"), r.get("week") lines[(ht, at, s, w)] = r k2 = (ht, at, s, None) if k2 not in lines: lines[k2] = r games = [g for g in games_raw if g.get("home_points") is not None] def payout_of(ml, won, bet=100): if not won: return -bet if ml < 0: return bet * (100 / abs(ml)) else: return bet * (ml / 100) picks = [] for game in games: ht, at = game["home_team"], game["away_team"] week, ns = game.get("week"), game.get("neutral_site", False) if week is None: continue ht_l, at_l = ht.strip().lower(), at.strip().lower() line = lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, week)) or lines.get((ht_l, at_l, season, None)) if not line: continue if use_opening_line: mkt_spread = line.get("opening_spread") if line.get("opening_spread") is not None else line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("opening_over_under") if line.get("opening_over_under") is not None else line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("opening_home_ml") if line.get("opening_home_ml") is not None else line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("opening_away_ml") if line.get("opening_away_ml") is not None else line.get("away_moneyline") else: mkt_spread = line.get("spread") mkt_total = line.get("over_under") home_ml = line.get("home_moneyline") away_ml = line.get("away_moneyline") sp = predict_sp_from_data(ht, at, season, ns, sp_ratings) if not sp: continue pm = sp["predicted_margin"] pred_total = sp.get("predicted_total") sp_win_prob_home = sp.get("win_prob_home") actual_margin = (game["home_points"] or 0) - (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_total = (game["home_points"] or 0) + (game["away_points"] or 0) actual_home_win = actual_margin > 0 pick = { "week": week, "home_team": ht, "away_team": at, "home_pts": game["home_points"], "away_pts": game["away_points"], "is_postseason": False, # could add postseason logic if needed } # ── SPREAD ── if mkt_spread is not None: pred_spread = -pm edge_val = abs(pred_spread - mkt_spread) abs_spread = abs(mkt_spread) pick_home = pred_spread < mkt_spread market_home_fav = mkt_spread < 0 sp_picked_fav = (pick_home and market_home_fav) or (not pick_home and not market_home_fav) push = actual_margin == -mkt_spread home_covered = actual_margin > -mkt_spread hit = None if push else (home_covered if pick_home else not home_covered) tier = None if abs_spread < 14 and edge_val >= 1: if sp_picked_fav: tier = "A+" elif edge_val >= 3.5: tier = "A" pick["spread"] = { "tier": tier, "pick_team": ht if pick_home else at, "line": mkt_spread if pick_home else -mkt_spread, "edge": round(edge_val, 1), "projection": f"{ht if pred_spread < 0 else at} by {abs(pred_spread):.1f}", "actual": f"{ht if actual_margin > 0 else at} by {abs(actual_margin)}", "hit": hit, "odds": -110, "pnl": 0 if hit is None else (90.91 if hit else -100), } # ── O/U ── if mkt_total is not None and pred_total is not None: edge_val = abs(pred_total - mkt_total) pick_over = pred_total > mkt_total if actual_total == mkt_total: hit = None else: hit = (actual_total > mkt_total) if pick_over else (actual_total < mkt_total) tier = None if mkt_total < 65 and edge_val >= 7: tier = "A+" elif mkt_total < 65 and edge_val >= 4: tier = "A" pick["ou"] = { "tier": tier, "pick": "Over" if pick_over else "Under", "total": mkt_total, "edge": round(edge_val, 1), "projection": f"{pred_total:.1f}", "actual": f"{actual_total}", "hit": hit, "odds": -110, "pnl": 90.91 if hit else (-100 if hit is False else 0), } # ── ML ── if home_ml is not None and away_ml is not None and sp_win_prob_home is not None: home_implied, away_implied = no_vig_prob(home_ml, away_ml) if home_implied is not None: he = sp_win_prob_home - home_implied ae = (1 - sp_win_prob_home) - away_implied side = None if he >= ae and he > 0: side, ml_edge, ml_impl, ml_price = "home", he, home_implied, home_ml elif ae > 0: side, ml_edge, ml_impl, ml_price = "away", ae, away_implied, away_ml if side: ml_hit = (side == "home") == actual_home_win payout = payout_of(ml_price, ml_hit, 100) ml_tier = None if ml_edge >= 0.10 and -300 <= ml_price <= 200: ml_tier = "smart_money" if ml_edge >= 0.15 and ml_price >= 150: ml_tier = "lottery_shot" pick["ml"] = { "tier": ml_tier, "pick_team": ht if side == "home" else at, "ml": ml_price, "edge": round(ml_edge, 3), "implied": round(ml_impl, 3), "projection": f"{round(sp_win_prob_home*100 if side == 'home' else (1-sp_win_prob_home)*100, 1)}% win prob", "actual": f"{ht if actual_margin > 0 else at} wins", "hit": ml_hit, "odds": ml_price, "pnl": round(payout, 2), } picks.append(pick) return picks def _format_bet(bet_type_name, bet_data, away_team, home_team): """Format a bet into the structure the frontend renders.""" return { "type": bet_type_name, "tier": bet_data.get("tier"), "pick": bet_data.get("pick") or bet_data.get("pick_team") or "", "edge":
