bet_data.get("edge"), "projection": bet_data.get("projection"), "actual": bet_data.get("actual"), "hit": bet_data.get("hit"), "odds": bet_data.get("odds"), "pnl": bet_data.get("pnl"), "away_team": away_team, "home_team": home_team, } def _build_weekly_response(picks, bet_extractor, bet_size=100, starting_bankroll=5000): """ Roll picks into a weekly response shape. bet_extractor(pick) returns a list of bet dicts to include for that game, or []. """ from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: bets = bet_extractor(p) for b in bets: by_week[p["week"]].append((p, b)) weeks_out = [] total_bets = 0 total_hits = 0 total_pnl = 0.0 bankroll = starting_bankroll for week_num in sorted(by_week.keys()): items = by_week[week_num] bets_detail = [] week_hits = 0 week_pnl = 0.0 for (p, b) in items: # Skip pushes/null hits but still display detail = _format_bet(b["type"], b, p["away_team"], p["home_team"]) bets_detail.append(detail) if b.get("hit") is True: week_hits += 1 total_hits += 1 week_pnl += (b.get("pnl") or 0) total_pnl += (b.get("pnl") or 0) total_bets += 1 bankroll += week_pnl weeks_out.append({ "week": week_num, "bets": len(items), "hits": week_hits, "hit_pct": round(week_hits / len(items) * 100, 1) if items else 0, "week_pnl": round(week_pnl, 2), "bankroll": round(bankroll, 2), "bets_detail": bets_detail, "is_postseason": False, }) total_bet = total_bets * bet_size return { "weekly": weeks_out, "total_bets": total_bets, "total_hits": total_hits, "hit_pct": round(total_hits / total_bets * 100, 1) if total_bets else 0, "total_profit": round(total_pnl, 2), "roi": round(total_pnl / total_bet * 100, 2) if total_bet else 0, } # ───── Endpoint: A+ Board (all A+ picks across spread/OU/ML for a season) ───── @app.get("/results/aplus-board") def results_aplus_board(season: int, bet_size: float = 100): """All A+ tier picks for a season, across spread, O/U, and ML.""" import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) def extract(pick): bets = [] if pick.get("spread", {}).get("tier") == "A+": bets.append({**pick["spread"], "type": "Spread"}) if pick.get("ou", {}).get("tier") == "A+": bets.append({**pick["ou"], "type": "O/U"}) if pick.get("ml", {}).get("tier") in ("smart_money", "lottery_shot"): # use the per-ML payout, not flat ml_bet = {**pick["ml"], "type": "ML"} bets.append(ml_bet) return bets return _build_weekly_response(picks, extract, bet_size=bet_size) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───── Endpoint: POTW (best A+ spread by edge per week) ───── @app.get("/results/potw") def results_potw(season: int, bet_size: float = 100): import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) # Group by week, pick highest-edge A+ spread per week from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: if p.get("spread", {}).get("tier") == "A+": by_week[p["week"]].append(p) chosen_picks = set() for week, ps in by_week.items(): best = max(ps, key=lambda x: x["spread"]["edge"]) chosen_picks.add(id(best)) def extract(pick): if id(pick) in chosen_picks: return [{**pick["spread"], "type": "Spread"}] return [] return _build_weekly_response(picks, extract, bet_size=bet_size) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───── Endpoint: ToTW (best A+ O/U by edge per week) ───── @app.get("/results/totw") def results_totw(season: int, bet_size: float = 100): import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: if p.get("ou", {}).get("tier") == "A+": by_week[p["week"]].append(p) chosen_picks = set() for week, ps in by_week.items(): best = max(ps, key=lambda x: x["ou"]["edge"]) chosen_picks.add(id(best)) def extract(pick): if id(pick) in chosen_picks: return [{**pick["ou"], "type": "O/U"}] return [] return _build_weekly_response(picks, extract, bet_size=bet_size) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───── Endpoint: Smart Money ML ───── @app.get("/results/smart-money") def results_smart_money(season: int, bet_size: float = 100): """Highest-confidence Smart Money ML per week — selected by implied probability.""" import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: if p.get("ml", {}).get("tier") == "smart_money": by_week[p["week"]].append(p) chosen_picks = set() for week, ps in by_week.items(): # Select by highest implied = most confident pick (matches unified backtest) best = max(ps, key=lambda x: x["ml"]["implied"]) chosen_picks.add(id(best)) def extract(pick): if id(pick) in chosen_picks: return [{**pick["ml"], "type": "ML"}] return [] return _build_weekly_response(picks, extract, bet_size=bet_size) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───── Endpoint: Lottery Shot ML ───── @app.get("/results/lottery-shot") def results_lottery_shot(season: int, bet_size: float = 100): """Highest-EV Lottery Shot ML per week — selected by expected dollar EV.""" import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: if p.get("ml", {}).get("tier") == "lottery_shot": by_week[p["week"]].append(p) def ev_of(p): ml = p["ml"] our_prob = ml["implied"] + ml["edge"] if ml["ml"] < 0: win_amt = 100 * (100 / abs(ml["ml"])) else: win_amt = 100 * (ml["ml"] / 100) return our_prob * win_amt - (1 - our_prob) * 100 chosen_picks = set() for week, ps in by_week.items(): best = max(ps, key=ev_of) chosen_picks.add(id(best)) def extract(pick): if id(pick) in chosen_picks: return [{**pick["ml"], "type": "ML"}] return [] return _build_weekly_response(picks, extract, bet_size=bet_size) except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()} # ───── Endpoint: Parlay (top 3 A+ spread+OU by edge per week, 3-leg parlay) ───── @app.get("/results/parlay") def results_parlay(season: int, bet_size: float = 100, parlay_payout_x: float = 6.0): import traceback try: picks = _build_results_picks(season) from collections import defaultdict by_week = defaultdict(list) for p in picks: # collect A+ spread + A+ OU candidates per game, with normalized edge # (edge above the tier's minimum threshold, so spread and OU edges # are comparable on the same scale) if p.get("spread", {}).get("tier") == "A+": spread_edge = p["spread"]["edge"] by_week[p["week"]].append({ "game": p, "leg_type": "Spread", "edge": spread_edge, "norm_edge": spread_edge - 1.0, # A+ spread minimum "leg": p["spread"] }) if p.get("ou", {}).get("tier") == "A+": ou_edge = p["ou"]["edge"] by_week[p["week"]].append({ "game": p, "leg_type": "O/U", "edge": ou_edge, "norm_edge": ou_edge - 7.0, # A+ O/U minimum "leg": p["ou"] }) weeks_out = [] total_parlays = 0 total_hits = 0 total_pnl = 0.0 bankroll = 5000 for week_num in sorted(by_week.keys()): cands = sorted(by_week[week_num], key=lambda c: -c["norm_edge"]) if len(cands) < 3: continue legs = cands[:3] all_hit = all(l["leg"]["hit"] == True for l in legs) week_pnl = bet_size * parlay_payout_x - bet_size if all_hit else -bet_size bets_detail = [] for l in legs: game = l["game"] bets_detail.append({ "type": l["leg_type"], "tier": "A+", "pick": l["leg"].get("pick") or l["leg"].get("pick_team") or "", "edge": l["edge"], "projection": l["leg"].get("projection"), "actual": l["leg"].get("actual"), "hit": l["leg"]["hit"], "odds": l["leg"].get("odds"), "pnl": 0, # parlay legs don't have individual pnl "away_team": game["away_team"], "home_team": game["home_team"], }) bankroll += week_pnl total_parlays += 1 if all_hit: total_hits += 1 total_pnl += week_pnl weeks_out.append({ "week": week_num, "bets": 3, "hits": sum(1 for l in legs if l["leg"]["hit"] == True), "hit_pct": 100.0 if all_hit else 0.0, "week_pnl": round(week_pnl, 2), "bankroll": round(bankroll, 2), "bets_detail": bets_detail, "is_postseason": False, "parlay_hit": all_hit, }) return { "weekly": weeks_out, "total_bets": total_parlays, "total_hits": total_hits, "hit_pct": round(total_hits / total_parlays * 100, 1) if total_parlays else 0, "total_profit": round(total_pnl, 2), "roi": round(total_pnl / (total_parlays * bet_size) * 100, 2) if total_parlays else 0, "parlay_payout_x": parlay_payout_x, } except Exception as e: return {"error": str(e), "traceback": traceback.format_exc()}
